<s> THE FIRM OF GIRDLESTONE </s>
<s> CHAPTER I </s>
<s> MR </s>
<s> JOHN HARSTON KEEPS AN APPOINTMENT </s>
<s> The approach to the offices of Girdlestone and Co </s>
<s> was not a very dignified one, nor would the uninitiated who traversed it form any conception of the commercial prosperity of the firm in question </s>
<s> Close to the corner of a broad and busy street, within a couple of hundred yards of Fenchurch Street Station, a narrow doorway opens into a long whitewashed passage </s>
<s> On one side of this is a brass plate with the inscription "Girdlestone and Co., African Merchants," and above it a curious hieroglyphic supposed to represent a human hand in the act of pointing </s>
<s> Following the guidance of this somewhat ghostly emblem, the wayfarer finds himself in a small square yard surrounded by doors, upon one of which the name of the firm reappears in large white letters, with the word "Push" printed beneath it </s>
<s> If he follows this laconic invitation he will make his way into a long, low apartment, which is the counting-house of the African traders </s>
<s> On the afternoon of which we speak things were quiet at the offices </s>
<s> The line of pigeon-holes in the wire curtain was deserted by the public, though the linoleum-covered floor bore abundant traces of a busy morning </s>
<s> Misty London light shone hazily through the glazed windows and cast dark shadows in the corners </s>
<s> On a high perch in the background a weary-faced, elderly man, with muttering lips and tapping fingers, cast up endless lines of figures </s>
<s> Beneath him, in front of two long shining mahogany desks, half a score of young men, with bent heads and stooping shoulders, appeared to be riding furiously, neck and neck, in the race of life </s>
<s> Any _habitue_ of a London office might have deduced from their relentless energy and incorruptible diligence that they were under the eyes of some member of the firm </s>
<s> The member in question was a broad-shouldered, bull-necked young man, who leaned against the marble mantel-piece, turning over the pages of an almanac, and taking from time to time a stealthy peep over the top of it at the toilers around him </s>
<s> Command was imprinted in every line of his strong, square-set face and erect, powerful frame </s>
<s> Above the medium size, with a vast spread of shoulder, a broad aggressive jaw, and bright bold glance, his whole pose and expression spoke of resolution pushed to the verge of obstinacy </s>
<s> There was something classical in the regular olive-tinted features and black, crisp, curling hair fitting tightly to the well-rounded head </s>
<s> Yet, though classical, there was an absence of spirituality </s>
<s> It was rather the profile of one of those Roman emperors, splendid in its animal strength, but lacking those subtle softnesses of eye and mouth which speak of an inner life </s>
<s> The heavy gold chain across the waistcoat and the bright stone which blazed upon the finger were the natural complement of the sensuous lip and curving chin </s>
<s> Such was Ezra, only child of John Girdlestone, and heir to the whole of his vast business </s>
<s> Little wonder that those who had an eye to the future bent over their ledgers and worked with a vigour calculated to attract the attention of the junior partner, and to impress him with a due sense of their enthusiastic regard for the interests of the firm </s>
<s> It was speedily apparent, however, that the young gentleman's estimate of their services was not entirely based upon their present performance </s>
<s> With his eyes still fixed upon the almanac and a sardonic smile upon his dark face, he uttered a single word-- "Parker" </s>
<s> A flaxen-haired clerk, perched at the further end of the high glistening desk, gave a violent start, and looked up with a scared face </s>
<s> "Well, Parker, who won" </s>
<s> asked the junior partner </s>
<s> "Won, sir" </s>
<s> the youth stammered </s>
<s> "Yes, who won" </s>
<s> repeated his employer </s>
<s> "I hardly understand you, sir," the clerk said, growing very red and confused </s>
<s> "Oh yes, you do, Parker," young Girdlestone remarked, tapping his almanac sharply with the paper-knife </s>
<s> "You were playing odd man out with Robson and Perkins when I came in from lunch </s>
<s> As I presume you were at it all the time I was away, I have a natural curiosity to know who won" </s>
<s> The three unhappy clerks fixed their eyes upon their ledgers to avoid the sarcastic gaze of their employer </s>
<s> He went on in the same quiet tones-- "You gentlemen draw about thirty shillings a week from the firm </s>
<s> I believe I am right in my figures, Mr Gilray" </s>
<s> addressing the senior clerk seated at the high solitary desk apart from the others </s>
<s> "Yes, I thought so </s>
<s> Now, odd man out is, no doubt, a very harmless and fascinating game, but you can hardly expect us to encourage it so far as to pay so much an hour for the privilege of having it played in our counting-house </s>
<s> I shall therefore recommend my father to deduct five shillings from the sum which each of you will receive upon Saturday </s>
<s> That will cover the time which you have devoted to your own amusements during the week" </s>
<s> He paused, and the three culprits were beginning to cool down and congratulate themselves, when he began again </s>
<s> "You will see, Mr Gilray, that this deduction is made," he said, "and at the same time I beg that you will deduct ten shillings from your own salary, since, as senior clerk, the responsibility of keeping order in this room in the absence of your employers rests with you, and you appear to have neglected it </s>
<s> I trust you will look to this, Mr Gilray" </s>
<s> "Yes, sir," the senior clerk answered meekly </s>
<s> He was an elderly man with a large family, and the lost ten shillings would make a difference to the Sunday dinner </s>
<s> There was nothing for it but to bow to the inevitable, and his little pinched face assumed an expression of gentle resignation </s>
<s> How to keep his ten young subordinates in order, however, was a problem which vexed him sorely </s>
<s> The junior partner was silent, and the remaining clerks were working uneasily, not exactly knowing whether they might not presently be included in the indictment </s>
<s> Their fears were terminated, however, by the sharp sound of a table-gong and the appearance of a boy with the announcement that Mr Girdlestone would like a moment's conversation with Mr Ezra </s>
<s> The latter gave a keen glance at his subjects and withdrew into the back office, a disappearance which was hailed by ten pens being thrown into the air and deftly caught again, while as many derisive and triumphant young men mocked at the imploring efforts of old Gilray in the interests of law and order </s>
<s> The sanctum of Mr John Girdlestone was approached by two doors, one of oak with ground-glass panels, and the other covered with green baize </s>
<s> The room itself was small, but lofty, and the walls were ornamented by numerous sections of ships stuck upon long flat boards, very much as the remains of fossil fish are exhibited in museums, together with maps, charts, photographs, and lists of sailings innumerable </s>
<s> Above the fire-place was a large water-colour painting of the barque _Belinda_ as she appeared when on a reef to the north of Cape Palmas </s>
<s> An inscription beneath this work of art announced that it had been painted by the second officer and presented by him to the head of the firm </s>
<s> It was generally rumoured that the merchants had lost heavily over this disaster, and there were some who quoted it as an instance of Girdlestone's habitual strength of mind that he should decorate his wall with so melancholy a souvenir </s>
<s> This view of the matter did not appear to commend itself to a flippant member of Lloyd's agency, who contrived to intimate, by a dexterous use of his left eyelid and right forefinger, that the vessel may not have been so much under-insured, nor the loss to the firm so enormous as was commonly reported </s>
<s> John Girdlestone, as he sat at his square office-table waiting for his son, was undeniably a remarkable-looking man </s>
<s> For good or for evil no weak character lay beneath that hard angular face, with the strongly marked features and deep-set eyes </s>
<s> He was clean shaven, save for an iron-grey fringe of ragged whisker under each ear, which blended with the grizzled hair above </s>
<s> So self-contained, hard-set, and immutable was his expression that it was impossible to read anything from it except sternness and resolution, qualities which are as likely to be associated with the highest natures as with the most dangerous </s>
<s> It may have been on account of this ambiguity of expression that the world's estimate of the old merchant was a very varying one </s>
<s> He was known to be a fanatic in religion, a purist in morals, and a man of the strictest commercial integrity </s>
<s> Yet there were some few who looked askance at him, and none, save one, who could apply the word "friend" to him </s>
<s> He rose and stood with his back to the fire-place as his son entered </s>
<s> He was so tall that he towered above the younger man, but the latter's square and compact frame made him, apart from the difference of age, the stronger man </s>
<s> The young man had dropped the air of sarcasm which he found was most effective with the clerks, and had resumed his natural manner, which was harsh and brusque </s>
<s> "What's up" </s>
<s> he asked, dropping back into a chair, and jingling the loose coins in his trouser pockets </s>
<s> "I have had news of the _Black Eagle_," his father answered </s>
<s> "She is reported from Madeira" </s>
<s> "Ah" </s>
<s> cried the junior partner eagerly </s>
<s> "What luck" </s>
<s> "She is full, or nearly so, according to Captain Hamilton Miggs' report" </s>
<s> "I wonder Miggs was able to send a report at all, and I wonder still more that you should put any faith in it," his son said impatiently </s>
<s> "The fellow is never sober" </s>
<s> "Miggs is a good seaman, and popular on the coast </s>
<s> He may indulge at times, but we all have our failings </s>
<s> Here is the list as vouched for by our agent </s>
<s> 'Six hundred barrels of palm oil'--" "Oil is down to-day," the other interrupted </s>
<s> "It will rise before the _Black Eagle_ arrives," the merchant rejoined confidently </s>
<s> "Then he has palm nuts in bulk, gum, ebony, skins, cochineal, and ivory" </s>
<s> The young man gave a whistle of satisfaction </s>
<s> "Not bad for old Miggs" </s>
<s> he said </s>
<s> "Ivory is at a fancy figure" </s>
<s> "We are sorely in need of a few good voyages," Girdlestone remarked, "for things have been very slack of late </s>
<s> There is one very sad piece of intelligence here which takes away the satisfaction which we might otherwise feel </s>
<s> Three of the crew have died of fever </s>
<s> He does not mention the names" </s>
<s> "The devil" </s>
<s> said Ezra </s>
<s> "We know very well what that means </s>
<s> Three women, each with an armful of brats, besieging the office and clamouring for a pension </s>
<s> Why are seamen such improvident dogs" </s>
<s> His father held up his white hand deprecatingly </s>
<s> "I wish," he said, "that you would treat these subjects with more reverence </s>
<s> What could be sadder than that the bread-winner of a family should be cut off </s>
<s> It has grieved me more than I can tell" </s>
<s> "Then you intend to pension the wives" </s>
<s> Ezra said, with a sly smile </s>
<s> "By no means," his father returned with decision </s>
<s> "Girdlestone and Co </s>
<s> are not an insurance office </s>
<s> The labourer is worthy of his hire, but when his work in this world is over, his family must fall back upon what has been saved by his industry and thrift </s>
<s> It would be a dangerous precedent for us to allow pensions to the wives of these sailors, for it would deprive the others of all motive for laying their money by, and would indirectly encourage vice and dissipation" </s>
<s> Ezra laughed, and continued to rattle his silver and keys </s>
<s> "It is not upon this matter that I desired to speak to you," Girdlestone continued </s>
<s> "It has, however, always been my practice to prefer matters of business to private affairs, however pressing </s>
<s> John Harston is said to be dying, and he has sent a message to me saying that he wishes to see me </s>
<s> It is inconvenient for me to leave the office, but I feel that it is my Christian duty to obey such a summons </s>
<s> I wish you, therefore, to look after things until I return" </s>
<s> "I can hardly believe that the news is true," Ezra said, in astonishment </s>
<s> "There must be some mistake </s>
<s> Why, I spoke to him on 'Change last Monday" </s>
<s> "It is very sudden," his father answered, taking his broad-brimmed hat from a peg </s>
<s> "There is no doubt about the fact, however </s>
<s> The doctor says that there is very little hope that he will survive until evening </s>
<s> It is a case of malignant typhoid" </s>
<s> "You are very old friends" </s>
<s> Ezra remarked, looking thoughtfully at his father </s>
<s> "I have known him since we were boys together," the other replied, with a slight dry cough, which was the highest note of his limited emotional gamut </s>
<s> "Your mother, Ezra, died upon the very day that Harston's wife gave birth to this daughter of his, seventeen years ago </s>
<s> Mrs Harston only survived a few days </s>
<s> I have heard him say that, perhaps, we should also go together </s>
<s> We are in the hands of a higher Power, however, and it seems that one shall be taken and another left" </s>
<s> "How will the money go if the doctors are right" </s>
<s> Ezra asked keenly </s>
<s> "Every penny to the girl </s>
<s> She will be an heiress </s>
<s> There are no other relations that I know of, except the Dimsdales, and they have a fair fortune of their own </s>
<s> But I must go" </s>
<s> "By the way, malignant typhoid is very catching, is it not" </s>
<s> "So they say," the merchant said quietly, and strode off through the counting-house </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone remained behind, stretching his legs In front of the empty grate </s>
<s> "The governor is a hard nail," he soliloquized, as he stared down at the shining steel bars </s>
<s> "Depend upon it, though, he feels this more than he shows </s>
<s> Why, it's the only friend he ever had in the world--or ever will have, in all probability </s>
<s> However, it's no business of mine," with which comforting reflection he began to whistle as he turned over the pages of the private day-book of the firm </s>
<s> It is possible that his son's surmise was right, and that the gaunt, unemotional African merchant felt an unwonted heartache as he hailed a hansom and drove out to his friend's house at Fulham </s>
<s> He and Harston had been charity schoolboys together, had roughed it together, risen together, and prospered together </s>
<s> When John Girdlestone was a raw-boned lad and Harston a chubby-faced urchin, the latter had come to look upon the other as his champion and guide </s>
<s> There are some minds which are parasitic in their nature </s>
<s> Alone they have little vitality, but they love to settle upon some stronger intellect, from which they may borrow their emotions and conclusions at second-hand </s>
<s> A strong, vigorous brain collects around it in time many others, whose mental processes are a feeble imitation of its own </s>
<s> Thus it came to pass that, as the years rolled on, Harston learned to lean more and more upon his old school-fellow, grafting many of his stern peculiarities upon his own simple vacuous nature, until he became a strange parody of the original </s>
<s> To him Girdlestone was the ideal man, Girdlestone's ways the correct ways, and Girdlestone's opinions the weightiest of all opinions </s>
<s> Forty years of this undeviating fidelity must, however he might conceal it, have made an impression upon the feelings of the elder man </s>
<s> Harston, by incessant attention to business and extreme parsimony, had succeeded in founding an export trading concern </s>
<s> In this he had followed the example of his friend </s>
<s> There was no fear of their interests ever coming into collision, as his operations were confined to the Mediterranean </s>
<s> The firm grew and prospered, until Harston began to be looked upon as a warm man in the City circles </s>
<s> His only child was Kate, a girl of seventeen </s>
<s> There were no other near relatives, save Dr </s>
<s> Dimsdale, a prosperous West-end physician </s>
<s> No wonder that Ezra Girdlestone's active business mind, and perhaps that of his father too, should speculate as to the disposal of the fortune of the dying man </s>
<s> Girdlestone pushed open the iron gate and strode down the gravel walk which led to his friend's house </s>
<s> A bright autumn sun shining out of a cloudless heaven bathed the green lawn and the many-coloured flower-beds in its golden light </s>
<s> The air, the leaves, the birds, all spoke of life </s>
<s> It was hard to think that death was closing its grip upon him who owned them all </s>
<s> A plump little gentleman in black was just descending the steps </s>
<s> "Well, doctor," the merchant asked, "how is your patient" </s>
<s> "You've not come with the intention of seeing him, have you" </s>
<s> the doctor asked, glancing up with some curiosity at the grey face and overhanging eyebrows of the merchant </s>
<s> "Yes, I am going up to him now" </s>
<s> "It is a most virulent case of typhoid </s>
<s> He may die in an hour or he may live until nightfall, but nothing can save him </s>
<s> He will hardly recognize you, I fear, and you can do him no good </s>
<s> It is most infectious, and you are incurring a needless danger </s>
<s> I should strongly recommend you not to go" </s>
<s> "Why, you've only just come down from him yourself, doctor" </s>
<s> "Ah, I'm there in the way of duty" </s>
<s> "So am I," said the visitor decisively, and passing up the stone steps of the entrance strode into the hall </s>
<s> There was a large sitting-room upon the ground floor, through the open door of which the visitor saw a sight which arrested him for a moment </s>
<s> A young girl was sitting in a recess near the window, with her lithe, supple figure bent forward, and her hands clasped at the back of her head, while her elbows rested upon a small table in front of her </s>
<s> Her superb brown hair fell in a thick wave on either side over her white round arms, and the graceful curve of her beautiful neck might have furnished a sculptor with a study for a mourning Madonna </s>
<s> The doctor had just broken his sad tidings to her, and she was still in the first paroxysm of her grief--a grief too acute, as was evident even to the unsentimental mind of the merchant, to allow of any attempt at consolation </s>
<s> A greyhound appeared to think differently, for he had placed his fore-paws upon his young mistress's lap, and was attempting to thrust his lean muzzle between her arms and to lick her face in token of canine sympathy </s>
<s> The merchant paused irresolutely for a moment, and then ascending the broad staircase he pushed open the door of Harston's room and entered </s>
<s> The blinds were drawn down and the chamber was very dark </s>
<s> A pungent whiff of disinfectants issued from it, mingled with the dank, heavy smell of disease </s>
<s> The bed was in a far corner </s>
<s> Without seeing him, Girdlestone could hear the fast laboured breathing of the invalid </s>
<s> A trimly dressed nurse who had been sitting by the bedside rose, and, recognizing the visitor, whispered a few words to him and left the room </s>
<s> He pulled the cord of the Venetian blind so as to admit a few rays of daylight </s>
<s> The great chamber looked dreary and bare, as carpet and hangings had been removed to lessen the chance of future infection </s>
<s> John Girdlestone stepped softly across to the bedside and sat down by his dying friend </s>
<s> The sufferer was lying on his back, apparently unconscious of all around him </s>
<s> His glazed eyes were turned upwards towards the ceiling, and his parched lips were parted, while the breath came in quick, spasmodic gasps </s>
<s> Even the unskilled eye of the merchant could tell that the angel of death was hovering very near him </s>
<s> With an ungainly attempt at tenderness, which had something pathetic in it, he moistened a sponge and passed it over the sick man's feverish brow </s>
<s> The latter turned his restless head round, and a gleam of recognition and gratitude came into his eyes </s>
<s> "I knew that you would come," he said </s>
<s> "Yes </s>
<s> I came the moment that I got your message" </s>
<s> "I am glad that you are here," the sufferer continued with a sigh of relief </s>
<s> From the brightened expression upon his pinched face, it seemed as if, even now in the jaws of death, he leaned upon his old schoolfellow and looked to him for assistance </s>
<s> He put a wasted hand above the counterpane and laid it upon Girdlestone's </s>
<s> "I wish to speak to you, John," he said </s>
<s> "I am very weak </s>
<s> Can you hear what I say" </s>
<s> "Yes, I hear you" </s>
<s> "Give me a spoonful from that bottle </s>
<s> It clears my mind for a time </s>
<s> I have been making my will, John" </s>
<s> "Yes," said the merchant, replacing the medicine bottle </s>
<s> "The lawyer made it this morning </s>
<s> Stoop your head and you will hear me better </s>
<s> I have less than fifty thousand </s>
<s> I should have done better had I retired years ago" </s>
<s> "I told you so," the other broke in gruffly </s>
<s> "You did--you did </s>
<s> But I acted for the best </s>
<s> Forty thousand I leave to my dear daughter Kate" </s>
<s> A look of interest came over Girdlestone's face </s>
<s> "And the balance" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "I leave that to be equally divided among the various London institutions for educating the poor </s>
<s> We were both poor boys ourselves, John, and we know the value of such schools" </s>
<s> Girdlestone looked perhaps a trifle disappointed </s>
<s> The sick man went on very slowly and painfully-- "My daughter will have forty thousand pounds </s>
<s> But it is so tied up that she can neither touch it herself nor enable any one else to do so until she is of age </s>
<s> She has no friends, John, and no relations, save only my cousin, Dr </s>
<s> George Dimsdale </s>
<s> Never was a girl left more lonely and unprotected </s>
<s> Take her, I beg of you, and bring her up under your own eye </s>
<s> Treat her as though she were your child </s>
<s> Guard her above all from those who would wreck her young life in order to share her fortune </s>
<s> Do this, old friend, and make me happy on my deathbed" </s>
<s> The merchant made no answer </s>

<s> CHAPTER III </s>
<s> THOMAS GILRAY MAKES AN INVESTMENT </s>
<s> The shambling little clerk was still standing at the door watching the retreating figure of the millionaire, and mentally splicing together his fragmentary remarks into a symmetrical piece of advice which might be carried home and digested at leisure, when his attention was attracted to a pale-faced woman, with a child in her arms, who was hanging about the entrance </s>

<s> CHAPTER IV </s>
<s> CAPTAIN HAMILTON MIGGS OF THE "BLACK EAGLE" </s>
<s> The head of the firm had hardly recovered his mental serenity after the painful duty of explaining her financial position to the Widow Hudson, when his quick ear caught the sound of a heavy footstep in the counting-house </s>
<s> A gruff voice was audible at the same time, which demanded in rather more energetic language than was usually employed in that orderly establishment, whether the principal was to be seen or not </s>
<s> The answer was evidently in the affirmative, for the lumbering tread came rapidly nearer, and a powerful double knock announced that the visitor was at the other side of the door </s>
<s> "Come in," cried Mr Girdlestone, laying down his pen </s>

<s> Nothing more substantial than a strong smell of spirituous liquors, however, entered the apartment </s>
<s> "Come in," the merchant repeated impatiently </s>

<s> Then a copper-coloured forehead appeared, with a couple of very shaggy eyebrows and eventually a pair of eyes, which protruded from their sockets and looked yellow and unhealthy </s>

<s> He was a stoutly-built sea-faring man, dressed in a pea jacket and blue trousers and holding his tarpaulin hat in his hand </s>

<s> "Why, captain," said the head of the firm, rising and grasping the other's hand with effusion, "I am glad to see you back safe and well" </s>
<s> "Glad to see ye, sir--glad to see ye" </s>
<s> His voice was thick and husky, and there was an indecision about his gait as though he had been drinking heavily </s>
<s> "I came in sort o' cautious," he continued, "'cause I didn't know who might be about </s>
<s> When you and me speaks together we likes to speak alone, you bet" </s>
<s> The merchant raised his bushy eyebrows a little, as though he did not relish the idea of mutual confidences suggested by his companion's remark </s>
<s> "Hadn't you better take a seat" </s>
<s> he said </s>
<s> The other took a cane-bottomed chair and carried it into the extreme corner of the office </s>
<s> Then having looked steadily at the wall behind him, and rapped it with his knuckles, he sat down, still throwing an occasional apprehensive glance over his shoulder </s>
<s> "I've got a touch of the jumps," he remarked apologetically to his employer </s>
<s> "I likes to _know_ as there ain't no one behind me" </s>
<s> "You should give up this shocking habit of drinking," Mr Girdlestone said seriously </s>
<s> "It is a waste of the best gifts with which Providence has endowed us </s>
<s> You are the worse for it both in this world and in the next" </s>
<s> Captain Hamilton Miggs did not seem to be at all impressed by this very sensible piece of advice </s>
<s> On the contrary, he chuckled boisterously to himself, and, slapping his thigh, expressed his opinion that his employer was a "rum 'un"--a conviction which he repeated to himself several times with various symptoms of admiration </s>
<s> "Well, well," Girdlestone said, after a short pause, "boys will be boys, and sailors, I suppose, will be sailors </s>
<s> After eight months of anxiety and toil, ending in success, captain--I am proud to be able to say the words--some little licence must be allowed </s>
<s> I do not judge others by the same hard and fast lines by which I regulate my own conduct" </s>
<s> This admirable sentiment also failed to elicit any response from the obdurate Miggs, except the same manifestations of mirth and the same audible aside as to the peculiarities of his master's character </s>
<s> "I must congratulate you on your cargo, and wish you the same luck for your next voyage," the merchant continued </s>
<s> "Ivory, an' gold dust, an' skins, an' resin, an' cochineal, an' gums, an' ebony, an' rice, an' tobacco, an' fruits, an' nuts in bulk </s>
<s> If there's a better cargo about, I'd like to see it," the sailor said defiantly </s>
<s> "An excellent cargo, captain; very good indeed </s>
<s> Three of your men died, I believe" </s>
<s> "Ay, three of the lubbers went under </s>
<s> Two o' fever and one o' snake-bite </s>
<s> It licks me what sailors are comin' to in these days </s>
<s> When I was afore the mast we'd ha' been ashamed to die o' a trifle like that </s>
<s> Look at me </s>
<s> I've been down wi' coast fever sixteen times, and I've had yellow jack an' dysentery, an' I've been bit by the black cobra in the Andamans </s>

<s> CHAPTER V </s>
<s> MODERN ATHENIANS </s>
<s> Edinburgh University may call herself with grim jocoseness the "alma mater" of her students, but if she be a mother at all she is one of a very heroic and Spartan cast, who conceals her maternal affection with remarkable success </s>
<s> The only signs of interest which she ever designs to evince towards her alumni are upon those not infrequent occasions when guineas are to be demanded from them </s>
<s> Then one is surprised to find how carefully the old hen has counted her chickens, and how promptly the demand is conveyed to each one of the thousands throughout the empire who, in spite of neglect, cherish a sneaking kindness for their old college </s>
<s> There is symbolism in the very look of her, square and massive, grim and grey, with never a pillar or carving to break the dead monotony of the great stone walls </s>
<s> She is learned, she is practical, and she is useful </s>
<s> There is little sentiment or romance in her composition, however, and in this she does but conform to the instincts of the nation of which she is the youngest but the most flourishing teacher </s>
<s> A lad coming up to an English University finds himself In an enlarged and enlightened public school </s>
<s> If he has passed through Harrow and Eton there is no very abrupt transition between the life which he has led in the sixth form and that which he finds awaiting him on the banks of the Cam and the Isis </s>
<s> Certain rooms are found for him which have been inhabited by generations of students in the past, and will be by as many in the future </s>
<s> His religion is cared for, and he is expected to put in an appearance at hall and at chapel </s>
<s> He must be within bounds at a fixed time </s>
<s> If he behave indecorously he is liable to be pounced upon and reported by special officials, and a code of punishments is hung perpetually over his head </s>
<s> In return for all this his University takes a keen interest in him </s>
<s> She pats him on the back if he succeeds </s>
<s> Prizes and scholarships, and fine fat fellowships are thrown plentifully in his way if he will gird up his loins and aspire to them </s>
<s> There is nothing of this in a Scotch University </s>
<s> The young aspirant pays his pound, and finds himself a student </s>
<s> After that he may do absolutely what he will </s>
<s> There are certain classes going on at certain hours, which he may attend if he choose </s>
<s> If not, he may stay away without the slightest remonstrance from the college </s>
<s> As to religion, he may worship the sun, or have a private fetish of his own upon the mantelpiece of his lodgings for all that the University cares </s>
<s> He may live where he likes, he may keep what hours he chooses, and he is at liberty to break every commandment in the decalogue as long as he behaves himself with some approach to decency within the academical precincts </s>
<s> In every way he is absolutely his own master </s>
<s> Examinations are periodically held, at which he may appear or not, as he chooses </s>
<s> The University is a great unsympathetic machine, taking in a stream of raw-boned cartilaginous youths at one end, and turning them out at the other as learned divines, astute lawyers, and skilful medical men </s>
<s> Of every thousand of the raw material about six hundred emerge at the other side </s>
<s> The remainder are broken in the process </s>
<s> The merits and faults of this Scotch system are alike evident </s>
<s> Left entirely to his own devices in a far from moral city, many a lad falls at the very starting-point of his life's race, never to rise again </s>
<s> Many become idlers or take to drink, while others, after wasting time and money which they could ill afford, leave the college with nothing learned save vice </s>
<s> On the other hand, those whose manliness and good sense keep them straight have gone through a training which lasts them for life </s>
<s> They have been tried, and have not been found wanting </s>
<s> They have learned self-reliance, confidence, and, in a word, have become men of the world while their _confreres_ in England are still magnified schoolboys </s>
<s> High up in a third flat in Howe Street one, Thomas Dimsdale, was going through his period of probation in a little bedroom and a large sitting-room, which latter, "more studentium," served the purpose of dining-room, parlour, and study </s>
<s> A dingy sideboard, with four still more dingy chairs and an archaeological sofa, made up the whole of the furniture, with the exception of a circular mahogany centre-table, littered with note-books and papers </s>
<s> Above the mantelpiece was a fly-blown mirror with innumerable cards and notices projecting in a fringe all around, and a pair of pipe racks flanking it on either side </s>
<s> Along the centre of the side-board, arranged with suspicious neatness, as though seldom disturbed, stood a line of solemn books, Holden's _Osteology_, Quain's _Anatomy_, Kirkes' _Physiology_, and Huxley's _Invertebrata_, together with a disarticulated human skull </s>
<s> On one side of the fireplace two thigh bones were stacked; on the other a pair of foils, two basket-hilted single-sticks, and a set of boxing-gloves </s>
<s> On a shelf in a convenient niche was a small stock of general literature, which appeared to have been considerably more thumbed than the works upon medicine </s>
<s> Thackeray's _Esmond_ and Meredith's _Richard Feveret_ rubbed covers with Irving's _Conquest of Granada_ and a tattered line of paper-covered novels </s>

<s> A large silver goblet, the trophy of that occasion, stood underneath upon a bracket </s>

<s> CHAPTER VI </s>
<s> A RECTORIAL ELECTION </s>
<s> It took some little time before his son, who was half-choked with laughter, could explain to the energetic doctor that the gentleman upon whom he was perched was not a dangerous lunatic, but, on the contrary, a very harmless and innocent member of society </s>

<s> A rectorial election is a peculiarly Scotch institution, and, however it may strike the impartial observer, it is regarded by the students themselves as a rite of extreme solemnity and importance from which grave issues may depend </s>
<s> To hear the speeches and addresses of rival orators one would suppose that the integrity of the constitution and the very existence of the empire hung upon the return of their special nominee </s>
<s> Two candidates are chosen from the most eminent of either party and a day is fixed for the polling </s>
<s> Every undergraduate has a vote, but the professors have no voice in the matter </s>
<s> As the duties are nominal and the position honourable, there is never any lack of distinguished aspirants for a vacancy </s>
<s> Occasionally some well-known literary or scientific man is invited to become a candidate, but as a rule the election is fought upon strictly political lines, with all the old-fashioned accompaniments of a Parliamentary contest </s>
<s> For months before the great day there is bustle and stir </s>
<s> Secret committees meet, rules are formulated, and insidious agents prowl about with an eye to the political training of those who have not yet nailed their colours to any particular mast </s>
<s> Then comes a grand meeting of the Liberal Students' Association, which is trumped by a dinner of the Undergraduates' Conservative Society </s>
<s> The campaign is then in full swing </s>
<s> Great boards appear at the University gates, on which pithy satires against one or other candidate, parodies on songs, quotations from their speeches, and gaudily painted cartoons are posted </s>
<s> Those who are supposed to be able to feel the pulse of the University move about with the weight of much knowledge upon their brows, throwing out hints as to the probable majority one way or the other </s>
<s> Some profess to know it to a nicety </s>
<s> Others shake their heads and remark vaguely that there is not much to choose either way </s>
<s> So week after week goes by, until the excitement reaches a climax when the date of the election comes round </s>
<s> There was no need upon that day for Dr </s>
<s> Dimsdale or any other stranger in the town to ask his way to the University, for the whooping and yelling which proceeded from that usually decorous building might have been heard from Prince's Street to Newington </s>
<s> In front of the gates was a dense crowd of townspeople peering through into the quadrangle, and deriving much entertainment from the movements of the lively young gentlemen within </s>
<s> Large numbers of the more peaceable undergraduates stood about under the arches, and these quickly made a way for the newcomers, for both Garraway and Dimsdale as noted athletes commanded a respect among their fellow-students which medallists and honours men might look for in vain </s>
<s> The broad open quadrangle, and all the numerous balconies and terraces which surround it, were crowded with an excited mob of students </s>
<s> The whole three thousand odd electors who stand upon the college rolls appeared to be present, and the noise which they were making would have reflected credit on treble their number </s>
<s> The dense crowd surged and seethed without pause or rest </s>

<s> The crowd was most dense and most noisy in front of the class-room in which the counting of the votes was going forward </s>
<s> At one the result was to be announced, and as the long hand of the great clock crept towards the hour, a hush of expectation fell upon the assembly </s>
<s> The brazen clang broke harshly out, and at the same moment the folding doors were flung open, and a knot of men rushed out into the crowd, who swirled and eddied round them </s>
<s> The centre of the throng was violently agitated, and the whole mass of people swayed outwards and inwards </s>

<s> Then the corner of a large placard was elevated above the heads of the rioters, on which was visible the word "Liberal" in great letters, but before it could be raised further it was torn down, and the struggle became fiercer than ever </s>
<s> Up came the placard again--the other corner this time--with the word "Majority" upon it, and then immediately vanished as before </s>

<s> CHAPTER VII </s>
<s> ENGLAND VERSUS SCOTLAND </s>
<s> The rectorial election had come and had gone, but another great event had taken its place </s>
<s> It was the day of the England and Scotland Rugby match </s>
<s> Better weather could not have been desired </s>
<s> The morning had been hazy, but as the sun shone out the fog had gradually risen, until now there remained but a suspicion of it, floating like a plume, above the frowning walls of Edinburgh Castle, and twining a fairy wreath round the unfinished columns of the national monument upon the Calton Hill </s>

<s> There were others besides the students who were excited about the coming struggle </s>
<s> All Edinburgh was in a ferment </s>
<s> Football is, and always has been, the national game of Scotland among those who affect violent exercise, while golf takes its place with the more sedately inclined </s>
<s> There is no game so fitted to appeal to a hardy and active people as that composite exercise prescribed by the Rugby Union, in which fifteen men pit strength, speed, endurance, and every manly attribute they possess in a prolonged struggle against fifteen antagonists </s>
<s> There is no room for mere knack or trickery </s>
<s> It is a fierce personal contest in which the ball is the central rallying point </s>
<s> That ball may be kicked, pushed, or carried; it may be forced onwards in any conceivable manner towards the enemy's goal </s>
<s> The fleet of foot may seize it and by superior speed thread their way through the ranks of their opponents </s>
<s> The heavy of frame may crush down all opposition by dead weight </s>
<s> The hardiest and most enduring must win </s>
<s> Even matches between prominent local clubs excite much interest in Edinburgh and attract crowds of spectators </s>
<s> How much more then when the pick of the manhood of Scotland were to try their strength against the very cream of the players from the South of the Tweed </s>
<s> The roads which converged on the Raeburn Place Grounds, on which the match was to be played, were dark with thousands all wending their way in one direction </s>
<s> So thick was the moving mass that the carriage of the Dimsdale party had to go at a walk for the latter half of the journey, In spite of the objurgations of the driver, who, as a patriot, felt the responsibility which rested upon him in having one of the team in his charge, and the necessity there was for delivering him up by the appointed time </s>
<s> Many in the crowd recognized the young fellow and waved their hands to him or called out a few words of encouragement </s>
<s> Miss Kate Harston and even the doctor began to reflect some of the interest and excitement which showed itself on every face around them </s>
<s> The youth alone seemed to be unaffected by the general enthusiasm, and spent the time in endeavouring to explain the principles of the game to his fair companion, whose ignorance of it was comprehensive and astounding </s>
<s> "You understand," he said, "that there are fifteen players on each side </s>
<s> But it would not do for the whole of these fifteen men to play in a crowd, for, in that case, if the other side forced the ball past them, they would have nothing to fall back upon--no reserves, as it were </s>
<s> Therefore, as we play the game in Scotland, ten men are told off to play in a knot </s>
<s> They are picked for their weight, strength, and endurance </s>
<s> They are called the forwards, and are supposed to be always on the ball, following it everywhere, never stopping or tiring </s>
<s> They are opposed, of course, by the forwards of the other side </s>
<s> Now, immediately behind the forwards are the two quarter-backs </s>
<s> They should be very active fellows, good dodgers and fast runners </s>
<s> They never join in the very rough work, but they always follow on the outskirts of the forwards, and if the ball is forced past it is their duty to pick it up and make away with it like lightning </s>
<s> If they are very fast they may succeed in carrying it a long way before they are caught--'tackled,' as we call it </s>
<s> It is their duty also to keep their eye on the quarter-backs of the enemy, and to tackle them if they get away </s>
<s> Behind them again are the two half-backs--or 'three-quarters,' as they call them in England </s>
<s> I am one of them </s>
<s> They are supposed to be fast runners too, and a good deal of the tackling comes to their lot, for a good runner of the other side can often get past the quarters, and then the halves have got to bring him down </s>
<s> Behind the half-backs is a single man--the back </s>
<s> He is the last resource when all others are past </s>
<s> He should be a sure and long kicker, so as to get the ball away from the goal by that means--but you are not listening" </s>
<s> "Oh yes, I am," said Kate </s>
<s> As a matter of fact the great throng and the novel sights were distracting her so much that she found it hard to attend to her companion's disquisition </s>
<s> "You'll understand it quickly enough when you see it," the student remarked cheerily </s>
<s> "Here we are at the grounds" </s>
<s> As he spoke the carriage rattled through a broad gateway into a large open grassy space, with a great pavilion at one side of it and a staked enclosure about two hundred yards long and a hundred broad, with a goal-post at each end </s>
<s> This space was marked out by gaily coloured flags, and on every side of it, pressing against the barrier the whole way round, was an enormous crowd, twenty and thirty deep, with others occupying every piece of rising ground or coign of vantage behind them </s>
<s> The most moderate computation would place the number of spectators at fifteen thousand </s>
<s> At one side there was a line of cabs in the background, and thither the carriage of the Dimsdales drove, while Tom rushed off with his bag to the pavilion to change </s>
<s> It was high time to do so, for just as the carriage took up its position a hoarse roar burst from the great multitude, and was taken up again and again </s>
<s> It was a welcome to the English team, which had just appeared upon the ground </s>
<s> There they were, clad in white knickerbockers and jerseys, with a single red rose embroidered upon their breasts; as gallant-looking a set of young fellows as the whole world could produce </s>
<s> Tall, square-shouldered, straight-limbed, as active as kittens and as powerful as young bullocks, it was clear that they would take a lot of beating </s>
<s> They were the pick of the University and London clubs, with a few players from the northern counties; not a man among them whose name was not known wherever football was played </s>
<s> That tall, long-legged youth is Evans, the great half-back, who is said to be able to send a drop-kick further than any of his predecessors in the annals of the game </s>
<s> There is Buller, the famous Cambridge quarter, only ten stone in weight, but as lithe and slippery as an eel; and Jackson, the other quarter, is just such another--hard to tackle himself, but as tenacious as a bulldog in holding an adversary </s>
<s> That one with the straw-coloured hair is Coles, the great forward; and there are nine lads of metal who will stand by him to-day through thick and thin </s>
<s> They were a formidable-looking lot, and betting, which had been five on four to them in the morning, showed symptoms of coming to five to three </s>
<s> In the meantime, by no means abashed at finding themselves the cynosure of so many eyes, the Englishmen proceeded to keep up their circulation by leap-frog and horse-play, for their jerseys were thin and the wind bleak </s>
<s> But where were their adversaries </s>
<s> A few impatient moments slowly passed, and then from one corner of the ground there rose a second cheer, which rippled down the long line of onlookers and swelled into a mighty shout as the Scotchmen vaulted over the barrier into the arena </s>
<s> It was a nice question for connoisseurs in physical beauty as to which team had the best of it in physique </s>
<s> The Northerners in their blue jerseys, with a thistle upon their breasts, were a sturdy, hard-bitten lot, averaging a couple of pounds more in weight than their opponents </s>
<s> The latter were, perhaps, more regularly and symmetrically built, and were pronounced by experts to be the faster team, but there was a massive, gaunt look about the Scotch forwards which promised well for their endurance </s>
<s> Indeed, it was on their forwards that they principally relied </s>
<s> The presence of three such players as Buller, Evans, and Jackson made the English exceptionally strong behind, but they had no men in front who were individually so strong and fast as Miller, Watts, or Grey </s>
<s> Dimsdale and Garraway, the Scotch half-backs, and Tookey, the quarter, whose blazing red head was a very oriflamme wherever the struggle waxed hottest, were the best men that the Northerners could boast of behind </s>
<s> The English had won the choice of goals, and elected to play with what slight wind there was at their backs </s>
<s> A small thing may turn the scale between two evenly balanced teams </s>
<s> Evans, the captain, placed the ball in front of him upon the ground, with his men lined all along on either side, as eager as hounds in leash </s>
<s> Some fifty yards in front of him, about the place where the ball would drop, the blue-vested Scots gathered in a sullen crowd </s>
<s> There was a sharp ring from a bell, a murmur of excitement from the crowd </s>
<s> Evans took two quick steps forward, and the yellow ball flew swift and straight, as if it had been shot from a cannon, right into the expectant group in front of him </s>
<s> For a moment there was grasping and turmoil among the Scotchmen </s>
<s> Then from the crowd emerged Grey, the great Glasgow forward, the ball tucked well under his arm, his head down, running like the wind, with his nine forwards in a dense clump behind him, ready to bear down all opposition, while the other five followed more slowly, covering a wider stretch of ground </s>
<s> He met the Englishmen who had started full cry after the ball the moment that their captain had kicked it </s>
<s> The first hurled himself upon him </s>
<s> Grey, without slackening his pace, swerved slightly, and he missed him </s>
<s> The second he passed in the same way, but the third caught quickly at his legs, and the Scot flew head over heels and was promptly collared </s>
<s> Not much use collaring him now </s>
<s> In the very act of falling he had thrown the ball behind him </s>
<s> Gordon, of Paisley, caught it and bore it on a dozen yards, when he was seized and knocked down, but not before he had bequeathed his trust to another, who struggled manfully for some paces before he too was brought to the ground </s>
<s> This pretty piece of "passing" had recovered for the Scotch all the advantage lost by the English kick-off, and was greeted by roars of applause from the crowd </s>
<s> And now there is a "maul" or "scrimmage" </s>
<s> Was there ever another race which did such things and called it play </s>
<s> Twenty young men, so blended and inextricably mixed that no one could assign the various arms and legs to their respective owners, are straining every muscle and fibre of their bodies against each other, and yet are so well balanced that the dense clump of humanity stands absolutely motionless </s>
<s> In the centre is an inextricable chaos where shoulders heave and heads rise and fall </s>
<s> At the edges are a fringe of legs--legs in an extreme state of tension-- ever pawing for a firmer foothold, and apparently completely independent of the rest of their owners, whose heads and bodies have bored their way Into the _melee_ </s>
<s> The pressure in there is tremendous, yet neither side gives an inch </s>
<s> Just on the skirts of the throng, with bent bodies and hands on knees, stand the cool little quarter-backs, watching the gasping giants, and also keeping a keen eye upon each other </s>
<s> Let the ball emerge near one of these, and he will whip it up and be ten paces off before those in the "maul" even know that it is gone </s>
<s> Behind them again are the halves, alert and watchful, while the back, with his hands in his pockets, has an easy consciousness that he will have plenty of warning before the ball can pass the four good men who stand between the "maul" and himself </s>
<s> Now the dense throng sways a little backwards and forwards </s>
<s> An inch is lost and an inch is gained </s>
<s> The crowd roar with delight </s>
<s> "Mauled, Scotland" </s>
<s> "Mauled England" </s>
<s> "England" </s>
<s> "Scotland" </s>

<s> A blue coat emerges among the white ones </s>

<s> There is no one in front of them, no one but a single little man, almost a boy in size and weight </s>

<s> shout the crowd </s>
<s> "Well run, Buller" </s>
<s> "Now, Tookey" </s>
<s> "Now, Dimsdale" </s>

<s> The little quarter-back had come to an end of his career, for Tom had been as quick as he and had caught him round the waist as he attempted to pass, and brought him to the ground </s>

<s> Dimsdale recovered himself first, however, and got past before the other had time to seize him </s>
<s> The goal was now not more than twenty yards off, with only one between Tom and it, though half a dozen more were in close pursuit </s>

<s> In the very act of falling he had managed to kick the ball, which flickered feebly up into the air and just cleared the English bar </s>

<s> Well, the breaking of a collar-bone is a small price to pay for the saving of such a match as that </s>
<s> So thought Tom Dimsdale as he made for the pavilion, with his father keeping off the exultant crowd upon one side and Jack Garraway upon the other </s>

<s> Within half an hour Tom was safely ensconced in the corner of the carriage, with his shoulder braced back, _secundum artem_, and his arm supported by a sling </s>
<s> How quietly and deftly the two women slipped a shawl here and a rug there to save him from the jarring of the carriage </s>
<s> It is part of the angel nature of woman that when youth and strength are maimed and helpless they appeal to her more than they can ever do in the pride and flush of their power </s>

<s> It had been an eventful day with the student </s>
<s> He had saved his side, he had broken his collar-bone, and now, most serious of all, he had realized that he was hopelessly in love </s>
<s> CHAPTER VIII </s>
<s> A FIRST PROFESSIONAL </s>
<s> Within a few weeks of his recovery from his accident Tom Dimsdale was to go up for his first professional examination, and his father, who had now retired from practice with a fair fortune, remained in Edinburgh until that event should come off </s>
<s> There had been some difficulty in persuading Girdlestone to give his consent to this prolongation of his ward's leave, but the old merchant was very much engrossed with his own affairs about that time, which made him more amenable than he might otherwise have been </s>
<s> The two travellers continued, therefore, to reside in their Princes Street hotel, but the student held on to his lodgings in Howe Street, where he used to read during the morning and afternoon </s>
<s> Every evening, however, he managed to dine at the _Royal_, and would stay there until his father packed him off to his books once more </s>
<s> It was in vain for him to protest and to plead for another half-hour </s>
<s> The physician was inexorable </s>
<s> When the fated hour came round the unhappy youth slowly gathered together his hat, his gloves, and his stick, spreading out that operation over the greatest possible extent of time which it could by any means be made to occupy </s>
<s> He would then ruefully bid his kinsfolk adieu, and retire rebelliously to his books </s>
<s> Very soon, however, he made a discovery </s>
<s> From a certain seat in the Princes Street Gardens it was possible to see the interior of the sitting-room in which the visitors remained after dinner </s>
<s> From the time when this fact dawned upon him, his rooms in the evening knew him no more </s>
<s> The gardens were locked at night, but that was a mere trifle </s>
<s> He used to scramble over the railings like a cat, and then, planting himself upon the particular seat, he would keep a watch upon the hotel window until the occupants of the room retired to rest </s>
<s> It might happen that his cousin remained invisible </s>
<s> Then he would return to his rooms in a highly dissatisfied state, and sit up half the night protesting against fate and smoking strong black tobacco </s>
<s> On the other hand, if he had the good luck to see the graceful figure of his old playfellow, he felt that that was the next best thing to being actually in her company, and departed eventually in a more contented frame of mind </s>
<s> Thus, when Dr </s>
<s> Dimsdale fondly imagined his son to be a mile away grappling with the mysteries of science, that undutiful lad was in reality perched within sixty yards of him, with his thoughts engrossed by very different matters </s>
<s> Kate could not fail to understand what was going on </s>
<s> However young and innocent a girl may be, there is always some subtle feminine instinct which warns her that she is loved </s>
<s> Then first she realizes that she has passed the shadowy frontier line which divides the child-life from that of the woman </s>
<s> Kate felt uneasy and perplexed, and half involuntarily she changed her manner towards him </s>
<s> It had been frank and sisterly; now it became more distant and constrained </s>
<s> He was quick to observe the change, and in private raved and raged at it </s>
<s> He even made the mistake of showing his pique to her, upon which she became still more retiring and conventional </s>
<s> Then be bemoaned himself in the sleepless watches of the night, and confided to his bed-post that in his belief such a case had never occurred before in the history of the world, and never by any chance could or would happen again </s>
<s> He also broke out into an eruption of bad verses, which were found by his landlady during her daily examination of his private papers, and were read aloud to a select audience of neighbours, who were all much impressed, and cackled sympathetically among themselves </s>
<s> By degrees Tom developed other symptoms of the distemper which had come upon him so suddenly </s>
<s> He had always been remarkable for a certain towsiness of appearance and carelessness of dress which harmonized with his Bohemian habits </s>
<s> All this he suddenly abjured </s>
<s> One fine morning he paid successive visits to his tailor, his boot-maker, his hatter, and his hosier, which left all those worthy tradesmen rubbing their hands with satisfaction </s>
<s> About a week afterwards he emerged from his rooms in a state of gorgeousness which impressed his landlady and amazed his friends </s>
<s> His old college companions hardly recognized Tom's honest phiz as it looked out above the most fashionable of coats and under the glossiest of hats </s>
<s> His father was anything but edified by the change </s>

<s> It is generally some comparative stranger who first makes that discovery and brings it home to friends and relatives </s>
<s> Love has an awkward way of intruding itself at inconvenient times, but it never came more inopportunely than when it smote one who was reading for his first professional examination </s>
<s> During these weeks, when Tom was stumping about in boots which were two sizes too small for him, in the hope of making his muscular, well-formed foot a trifle more elegant, and was splitting gloves in a way which surprised his glover, all his energies ought by rights to have been concentrated upon the mysteries of botany, chemistry, and zoology </s>

<s> The _viva voce_ ordeal was the one, however, which he knew would be most dangerous to him, and he dreaded it accordingly </s>

<s> CHAPTER IX </s>
<s> A NASTY CROPPER </s>
<s> But there were pitfalls ahead </s>
<s> As he moved to the botany table a grey-bearded examiner waved his hand in the direction of the row of microscopes as an intimation that the student was to look through them and pronounce upon what he saw </s>
<s> Tom seemed to compress his whole soul into his one eye as he glared hopelessly through the tube at what appeared to him to resemble nothing so much as a sheet of ice with the marks of skates upon it </s>

<s> the examiner growled impatiently </s>
<s> Courtesy is conspicuous by its absence in most of the Edinburgh examinations </s>
<s> "You must pass on to the next one, unless you can offer an opinion" </s>
<s> This venerable teacher of botany, though naturally a kind-hearted man, was well known as one of the most malignant species of examiners, one of the school which considers such an ordeal in the light of a trial of strength between their pupils and themselves </s>
<s> In his eyes the candidate was endeavouring to pass, and his duty was to endeavour to prevent him, a result which, in a large proportion of cases, he successfully accomplished </s>

<s> he reiterated fussily </s>

<s> "You've made a bad mistake, sir; a very bad one, indeed </s>

<s> CHAPTER X </s>
<s> DWELLERS IN BOHEMIA </s>
<s> The residence of Major Tobias Clutterbuck, late of the 119th Light Infantry, was not known to any of his friends </s>
<s> It is true that at times he alluded in a modest way to his "little place," and even went to the length of remarking airily to new acquaintances that he hoped they would look him up any time they happened to be in his direction </s>
<s> As he carefully refrained, however, from ever giving the slightest indication of which direction that might be, his invitations never led to any practical results </s>
<s> Still they had the effect of filling the recipient with a vague sense of proffered hospitality, and occasionally led to more substantial kindness in return </s>
<s> The gallant major's figure was a familiar one in the card-room of the _Rag and Bobtail_, at the bow-window of the Jeunesse Doree </s>
<s> Tall and pompous, with a portly frame and a puffy clean-shaven face which peered over an abnormally high collar and old-fashioned linen cravat, he stood as a very type and emblem of staid middle-aged respectability </s>
<s> The major's hat was always of the glossiest, the major's coat was without a wrinkle, and, in short, from the summit of the major's bald head to his bulbous finger-tips and his gouty toes, there was not a flaw which the most severe critic of deportment--even the illustrious Turveydrop himself--could have detected </s>
<s> Let us add that the conversation of the major was as irreproachable as his person--that he was a distinguished soldier and an accomplished traveller, with a retentive memory and a mind stuffed with the good things of a lifetime </s>
<s> Combine all these qualities, and one would naturally regard the major as a most desirable acquaintance </s>
<s> It is painful to have to remark, however, that, self-evident as this proposition might appear, it was vehemently contradicted by some of the initiated </s>
<s> There were rumours concerning the major which seriously compromised his private character </s>
<s> Indeed, such a pitch had they reached that when that gallant officer put himself forward as a candidate for a certain select club, he had, although proposed by a lord and seconded by a baronet, been most ignominiously pilled </s>
<s> In public the major affected to laugh over this social failure, and to regard it as somewhat in the nature of a practical joke, but privately he was deeply incensed </s>
<s> One day he momentarily dropped his veil of unconcern while playing billiards with the Honourable Fungus Brown, who was generally credited with having had some hand in the major's exclusion </s>
<s> "Be Ged </s>
<s> sir," the veteran suddenly exclaimed, inflating his chest and turning his apoplectic face upon his companion, "in the old days I would have called the lot of you out, sir, every demned one, beginning with the committee and working down; I would, be George" </s>
<s> At which savage attack the Honourable Fungus's face grew as white as the major's was red, and he began to wish that he had been more reserved in his confidences to some of his acquaintances respecting the exclusiveness of the club in question, or at least refrained from holding up the major's pilling as a proof thereof </s>
<s> The cause of this vague feeling of distrust which had gone abroad concerning the old soldier was no very easy matter to define </s>
<s> It is true that he was known to have a book on every race, and to have secret means of information from stud-grooms and jockeys which occasionally stood him in good stead; but this was no uncommon thing among the men with whom he consorted </s>
<s> Again, it is true that Major Clutterbuck was much addicted to whist, with guinea points, and to billiard matches for substantial sums, but these stimulating recreations are also habitual to many men who have led eventful lives and require a strong seasoning to make ordinary existence endurable </s>
<s> Perhaps one reason may have been that the major's billiard play in public varied to an extraordinary degree, so that on different occasions he had appeared to be aiming at the process termed by the initiated "getting on the money" </s>
<s> The warm friendships, too, which the old soldier had contracted with sundry vacuous and sappy youths, who were kindly piloted by him into quasi-fashionable life and shown how and when to spend their money, had been most uncharitably commented upon </s>
<s> Perhaps the vagueness about the major's private residence and the mystery which hung over him outside his clubs may also have excited prejudice against him </s>
<s> Still, however his detractors might malign him, they could not attempt to deny the fact that Tobias Clutterbuck was the third son of the Honourable Charles Clutterbuck, who again was the second son of the Earl of Dunross, one of the most ancient of Hibernian families </s>
<s> This pedigree the old soldier took care to explain to every one about him, more particularly to the sappy youths aforementioned </s>
<s> It chanced that on the afternoon of which we speak the major was engrossed by this very subject </s>

<s> CHAPTER XI </s>
<s> SENIOR AND JUNIOR </s>
<s> Although not a whisper had been heard of it in ordinary commercial circles, there was some foundation for the forecast which Von Baumser had made as to the fate of the great house of Girdlestone </s>
<s> For some time back matters had been going badly with the African traders </s>
<s> If the shrewd eyes of Major Tobias Clutterbuck were unable to detect any indications of this state of affairs in the manner or conversation of the junior partner, the reason simply was that that gentleman was entirely ignorant of the imminent danger which hung over his head </s>
<s> As far as he knew, the concern was as prosperous and as flourishing as it had been at the time of the death of John Harston </s>
<s> The momentous secret was locked in the breast of his grim old father, who bore it about with him as the Spartan lad did the fox--without a quiver or groan to indicate the care which was gnawing at his heart </s>
<s> Placed face to face with ruin, Girdlestone fought against it desperately, and, withal, coolly and warily, throwing away no chance and leaving no stone unturned </s>
<s> Above all, he exerted himself--and exerted himself successfully--to prevent any rumour of the critical position of the firm from leaking out in the city </s>
<s> He knew well that should that once occur nothing could save him </s>
<s> As the wounded buffalo is gored to death by the herd, so the crippled man of business may give up all hope when once his position is known by his fellows </s>
<s> At present, although Von Baumser and a few other such Ishmaelites might have an inkling from sources of their own as to how matters stood, the name of Girdlestone was still regarded by business men as the very synonym for commercial integrity and stability </s>
<s> If anything, there seemed to be more business in Fenchurch Street and more luxury at the residence at Eccleston Square than in former days </s>
<s> Only the stern-faced and silent senior partner knew how thin the veneer was which shone so deceptively upon the surface </s>
<s> Many things had contributed towards this state of affairs </s>
<s> The firm had been involved in a succession of misfortunes, some known to the world, and others known to no one save the elder Girdlestone </s>
<s> The former had been accepted with such perfect stoicism and cheerfulness that they rather increased than diminished the reputation of the concern; the latter were the more crushing, and also the more difficult to bear </s>
<s> Lines of fine vessels from Liverpool and from Hamburg were running to the West Coast of Africa, and competition had cut down freightage to the lowest possible point </s>
<s> Where the Girdlestones had once held almost a monopoly there were now many in the field </s>
<s> Again, the negroes of the coast were becoming educated and had a keen eye to business, so that the old profits were no longer obtainable </s>
<s> The days had gone by when flint-lock guns and Manchester prints could be weighed in the balance against ivory and gold dust </s>
<s> While these general causes were at work a special misfortune had befallen the house of Girdlestone </s>
<s> Finding that their fleet of old sailing vessels was too slow and clumsy to compete with more modern ships, they had bought in two first-rate steamers </s>
<s> One was the _Providence_, a fine screw vessel of twelve hundred tons, and the other was the _Evening Star_, somewhat smaller in size, but both classed A1 at Lloyd's </s>
<s> The former cost twenty-two thousand pounds, and the latter seventeen thousand </s>
<s> Now, Mr Girdlestone had always had a weakness for petty savings, and in this instance he determined not to insure his new vessels </s>
<s> If the crazy old tubs, for which he had paid fancy premiums for so many years with an eye to an ultimate profit, met with no disaster, surely those new powerful clippers were safe </s>
<s> With their tonnage and horse-power they appeared to him to be superior to all the dangers of the deep </s>
<s> It chanced, however, by that strange luck which would almost make one believe that matters nautical were at the mercy of some particularly malignant demon, that as the _Evening Star_ was steaming up Channel in a dense fog on her return from her second voyage, she ran right into the _Providence_, which had started that very morning from Liverpool upon her third outward trip </s>
<s> The _Providence_ was almost cut in two, and sank within five minutes, taking down the captain and six of the crew, while the _Evening Star_ was so much damaged about the bows that she put into Falmouth in a sinking condition </s>
<s> That day's work cost the African firm more than five and thirty thousand pounds </s>
<s> Other mishaps had occurred to weaken the firm, apart from their trade with the coast </s>
<s> The senior partner had engaged in speculation without the knowledge of his son, and the result had been disastrous </s>
<s> One of the Cornish tin mines in which he had sunk a large amount of money, and which had hitherto yielded him a handsome return, became suddenly exhausted, and the shares went down to zero </s>
<s> No firm could stand against such a run of bad luck, and the African trading company reeled before it </s>
<s> John Girdlestone had not said a word yet of all this to his son </s>
<s> As claims arose he settled them in the best manner he could, and postponed the inevitable day when he should have to give a true account of their financial position </s>
<s> He hoped against hope that the chapter of accidents or the arrival of some brilliant cargoes from the coast might set the concern on its legs again </s>
<s> From day to day he had been expecting news of one of his vessels </s>
<s> At last one morning he found a telegram awaiting him at the office </s>
<s> He tore it eagerly open, for it bore the Madeira mark </s>
<s> It was from his agent, Jose Alveciras, and announced that the voyage from which he had hoped so much had been a total failure </s>
<s> The cargo was hardly sufficient to defray the working expenses </s>
<s> As the merchant read it, his head dropped over the table and he groaned aloud </s>
<s> Another of the props which upheld him from ruin had snapped beneath him </s>
<s> There were three letters lying beside the telegram </s>
<s> He glanced through them, but there was no consolation in any of them </s>
<s> One was from a bank manager, informing him that his account was somewhat overdrawn </s>
<s> Another from Lloyd's Insurance Agency, pointing out that the policies on two of his vessels would lapse unless paid within a certain date </s>
<s> The clouds were gathering very darkly over the African firm, yet the old man bore up against misfortune with dauntless courage </s>
<s> He sat alone in his little room, with his head sunk upon his breast, and his thatched eye-brows drawn down over his keen grey eyes </s>
<s> It was clear to him that the time had come when he must enlighten his son as to the true state of their affairs </s>
<s> With his co-operation he might carry out a plan which had been maturing some months in his brain </s>
<s> It was a hard task for the proud and austere merchant to be compelled to confess to his son that he had speculated without his knowledge in the capital of the company, and that a large part of that capital had disappeared </s>
<s> These speculations in many instances had promised large returns, and John Girdlestone had withdrawn money from safer concerns, and reinvested it in the hope of getting a higher rate of interest </s>
<s> He had done this with his eyes open to the risk, and knowing that his son was of too practical and cautious a nature to embark in such commercial gambling, he had never consulted him upon the point, nor had he made any entry of the money so invested in the accounts of the firm </s>
<s> Hence Ezra was entirely ignorant of the danger which hung over them, and his father saw that, in order to secure his energetic assistance in the stroke which he was contemplating, it was absolutely necessary that he should know how critical their position was </s>

<s> CHAPTER XII </s>
<s> A CORNER IN DIAMONDS </s>
<s> John Girdlestone propounded his intention with such dignity and emphasis that he evidently expected the announcement to come as a surprise upon his son </s>

<s> The instant such a thing gets wind the value of the stones goes down wonderfully </s>
<s> The discovery of diamonds in Central India not long ago had that effect very markedly, and they have never recovered their value since </s>

<s> CHAPTER XIII </s>
<s> SHADOW AND LIGHT </s>
<s> John Girdlestone's private residence in Eccleston Square was a large and substantial house in a district which the wave of fashion had passed over in its westward course </s>
<s> It might still, however, be said to be covered by a deposit of eminent respectability </s>
<s> The building was stern and hard, and massive in its external appearance, but the interior was luxury itself, for the old merchant, in spite of his ascetic appearance, was inclined to be a sybarite at heart, and had a due appreciation of the good things of this world </s>
<s> Indeed, there was an oriental and almost barbarous splendour about the great rooms, where the richest of furniture was interspersed with skins from the Gaboon, hand-worked ivory from Old Calabar, and the thousand other strange valuables which were presented by his agents to the African trader </s>
<s> After the death of his friend, Girdlestone had been as good as his word </s>
<s> He had taken Kate Harston away from the desolate house at Fulham and brought her to live with him </s>
<s> From the garrets of that palatial edifice to the cellars she was at liberty to roam where she would, and do what she chose </s>
<s> The square garden too, with its smoke-dried trees and faded lawn, was at her disposal, in which she might walk, or work, or read </s>
<s> No cares or responsibilities were imposed upon her </s>
<s> The domestic affairs were superintended by a stern housekeeper, who bore a quaint resemblance to Girdlestone himself in petticoats, and who arranged every detail of housekeeping </s>
<s> The young girl had apparently only to exist and to be happy </s>
<s> Yet the latter item was not so easy as it might seem </s>
<s> It was not a congenial atmosphere </s>
<s> Her whole society consisted of the stern, unemotional merchant and his vulgar, occasionally brutal, son </s>
<s> At first, while the memory of her father was still fresh, she felt her new surroundings acutely, contrasting, as they did, with her happy Fulham home </s>
<s> Gradually, however, as time deadened the sting, she came to accommodate herself to circumstances </s>
<s> The two men left her very much to her own devices </s>
<s> Girdlestone was so engrossed in his business that he had little time to inquire into her pursuits, and Ezra, being addicted to late hours, was seldom seen except at breakfast-time, when she listened with awe to his sporting slang and cynical comments upon men and manners </s>

<s> CHAPTER XIV </s>
<s> A SLIGHT MISUNDERSTANDING </s>
<s> The revelation of the real state of the firm's finances was a terrible blow to Ezra Girdlestone </s>
<s> To a man of his overbearing, tempestuous disposition failure and poverty were bitter things to face </s>
<s> He had been wont to tread down before him all such little difficulties and obstacles as came across him in his former life </s>
<s> Now he encountered a great barrier which could not be passed so easily, and he raged and chafed before it </s>
<s> It made him still more wroth to think that the fault was none of his </s>
<s> All his life he had reckoned, as a matter of course, that when his father passed away he would be left almost a millionaire </s>

<s> He saw clearly that only a bold stroke could save them </s>
<s> He therefore threw himself heart and soul into the diamond scheme, and worked out the details in a masterly manner </s>

<s> CHAPTER XV </s>
<s> AN ADDITION TO THE HOUSE </s>
<s> There were rejoicings in Phillimore Gardens over Tom's engagement, for the two old people were both heartily fond of Kate--"our Kate," as they were wont proudly to call her </s>
<s> The physician chafed at first over the idea of keeping the matter a secret from Girdlestone </s>
<s> A little reflection served to show him, however, that there was nothing to be gained by informing him, while Kate's life, during the time that she was forced to remain under his roof, would be more tolerable as long as he was kept in ignorance of it </s>
<s> In the meanwhile the lovers saw little of each other, and Tom was only consoled by the thought that every day which passed brought him nearer to the time when he could claim his prize without concealment or fear </s>
<s> He went about as happy and as light-hearted a man as any in all London </s>
<s> His mother was delighted at his high spirits, but his bluff old father was not so well satisfied </s>
<s> "Confound the lad" </s>
<s> he said to himself </s>
<s> "He is settling down to a life of idleness </s>
