<s> CHAPTER XVI </s>
<s> THE FIRST STEP </s>
<s> It was a proud day for the ex-medical student when he first entered the counting-house of the African firm and realized that he was one of the governing powers in that busy establishment </s>
<s> Tom Dimsdale's mind was an intensely practical one, and although he had found the study of science an irksome matter, he was able to throw himself into business with uncommon energy and devotion </s>
<s> The clerks soon found that the sunburnt, athletic-looking young man intended to be anything but a sleeping partner, and both they and old Gilray respected him accordingly </s>
<s> The latter had at first been inclined to resent the new arrangement as far as his gentle down-trodden nature could resent anything </s>
<s> Hitherto he had been the monarch of the counting-house in the absence of the Girdlestones, but now a higher desk had been erected in a more central portion of the room, and this was for the accommodation of the new comer </s>
<s> Gilray, after his thirty years of service, felt this usurpation of his rights very keenly; but there was such a simple kindness about the invader, and he was so grateful for any assistance in his new duties, that the old clerk's resentment soon melted away </s>
<s> A little incident occurred which strengthened this kindly feeling </s>
<s> It chanced that some few days after Tom's first appearance in the office several of the clerks, who had not yet quite gauged what manner of man this young gentleman might be, took advantage of the absence of the Girdlestones to take a rise out of the manager </s>
<s> One of them, a great rawboned Scotchman, named McCalister, after one or two minor exhibitions of wit concluded by dropping a heavy ruler over the partition of the old man's desk in such a way that it crashed down upon his head as he sat stooping over his writing </s>
<s> Tom, who had been watching the proceedings with a baleful eye, sprang off his stool and made across the office at the offender </s>
<s> McCalister seemed inclined for a moment to brazen it out, but there was a dangerous sling about Tom's shoulders and a flush of honest indignation upon his face </s>
<s> "I didn't mean to hurt him," said the Scotchman </s>
<s> "Don't hit him, sir" </s>
<s> cried the little manager </s>
<s> "Beg his pardon," said Tom between his teeth </s>
<s> McCalister stammered out some lame apology, and the matter was ended </s>
<s> It revealed the new partner, however, in an entirely novel light to the inmates of the counting-house </s>
<s> That under such circumstances a complaint should be carried to the senior was only natural, but that the junior should actually take the matter into his own hands and execute lynch law then and there was altogether a new phenomenon </s>
<s> From that day Tom acquired a great ascendancy in the office, and Gilray became his devoted slave </s>
<s> This friendship with the old clerk proved to be very useful, for by means of his shrewd hints and patient teaching the new comer gained a grasp of the business which he could not have attained by any other method </s>
<s> Girdlestone called him into the office one day and congratulated him upon the progress which he was making </s>
<s> "My dear young man," he said to him in his patriarchal way, "I am delighted to hear of the way in which you identify yourself with the interests of the firm </s>

<s> "There is nothing I desire better," said Tom </s>
<s> "In addition to the routine of office work, and the superintendence of the clerks, I should wish you to have a thorough grasp of all the details of the shipping, and of the loading and unloading of our vessels, as well as of the storage of goods when landed </s>
<s> When any of our ships are in, I should wish you to go down to the docks and to overlook everything which is done" </s>

<s> "As you grow older," said the senior partner, "you will find it of inestimable value that you have had practical experience of what your subordinates have to do </s>
<s> My whole life has taught me that </s>

<s> He is a young man whom you might well take as an example, for he has great business capacity </s>

<s> Very much astonished would both of them have been had they realized that the working expenses were at present being paid entirely from their own capital until such time as the plot should ripen which was to restore the fortunes of the African company </s>

<s> CHAPTER XVII </s>
<s> THE LAND OF DIAMONDS </s>
<s> The anxious father had not very long to wait before he heard tidings of his son </s>
<s> Upon the first of June the great vessel weighed her anchor in the Southampton Water, and steamed past the Needles into the Channel </s>
<s> On the 5th she was reported from Madeira, and the merchant received telegrams both from the agent of the firm and from his son </s>
<s> Then there was a long interval of silence, for the telegraph did not extend to the Cape at that time, but, at last on the 8th of August, a letter announced Ezra's safe arrival </s>
<s> He wrote again from Wellington, which was the railway terminus, and finally there came a long epistle from Kimberley, the capital of the mining district, in which the young man described his eight hundred miles drive up country and all the adventures which overtook him on the way </s>
<s> "This place, Kimberley," he said in his letter, "has grown into a fair-sized town, though a few years ago it was just a camp </s>
<s> Now there are churches, banks, and a club in it </s>
<s> There are a sprinkling of well-dressed people in the streets, but the majority are grimy-looking chaps from the diggings, with slouched hats and coloured shirts, rough fellows to look at, though quiet enough as a rule </s>
<s> Of course, there are blacks everywhere, of all shades, from pure jet up to the lightest yellow </s>
<s> Some of these niggers have money, and are quite independent </s>
<s> You would be surprised at their impertinence </s>
<s> I kicked one of them in the hotel yesterday, and he asked me what the devil I was doing, so I knocked the insolent scoundrel down </s>
<s> He says that he will sue me, but I cannot believe that the law is so servile as to bolster up a black man against a white one </s>
<s> "Though Kimberley is the capital of the dry diggings, it is not there that all the actual mining is done </s>
<s> It goes on briskly in a lot of little camps, which are dotted along the Vaal River for fifty or sixty miles </s>
<s> The stones are generally bought by licensed agents immediately after they have been found, and are paid for by cheques on banks in Kimberley </s>
<s> I have, therefore, transferred our money to the Standard Bank here, and have taken my licence </s>
<s> I start to-morrow for Hebron, Klipdrift, and other of the mining centres to see for myself how business is done and to make friends with the miners, so as to get myself known </s>
<s> As soon as the news comes I shall buy in all that offers </s>
<s> Keep your eyes on that fellow Dimsdale, and let him know nothing of what is going on" </s>

<s> The men dig pits in loose gravel lying along the banks of the river, and it is in these pits that the diamonds are found </s>
<s> The black men, or 'boys,' as they call them, do all the work, and the 'baas,' or master, superintends </s>
<s> Everything that turns up belongs to the 'baas,' but the boys have a fixed rate of wages, which never varies, whether the work is paying or not </s>
<s> I was standing at Hebron watching one of the gangs working when the white chap gave a shout, and dived his hand into a heap of stuff he had just turned over, pulling out a dirty looking little lump about the size of a marble </s>
<s> At his shout all the other fellows from every claim within hearing gathered round, until there was quite a crowd </s>
<s> "'It's a fine stone,' said the man that turned it up </s>
<s> "'Fifty carats if it's one,' cried another, weighing it in the palm of his hand </s>
<s> "I had my scales with me, so I offered to weigh it </s>
<s> It was sixty-four and a half carats </s>
<s> Then they washed it and examined it </s>
<s> There was a lot of whispering among them and then the one who had found it came forward </s>
<s> "'You deal, don't you, Mr Girdlestone' </s>
<s> he said </s>
<s> "'Now and then,' I answered, 'but I'm not very keen about it </s>
<s> I came out here more for pleasure than business </s>

<s> There are two shades of yellow in it </s>
<s> It is worth little or nothing' </s>

<s> On descending the landlady discovered that the author of this disturbance was a fashionably dressed gentleman, who, upon closer inspection, proved to her great surprise to be none other than the usually demure part proprietor of her fourth floor </s>
<s> As to the major, he walked in quietly the next day about twelve o'clock, looking as trim and neat as ever, but minus the balance of the fifty pounds, nor did he think fit ever to make any allusion to this some what heavy deficit </s>
<s> CHAPTER XIX </s>
<s> NEWS FROM THE URALS </s>
<s> Major Tobias Clutterbuck had naturally reckoned that the longer he withheld this trump card of his the greater would be its effect when played </s>
<s> An obstacle appearing at the last moment produces more consternation than when a scheme is still in its infancy </s>
<s> It proved, however, that he had only just levied his blackmail in time, for within a couple of days of his interview with the head of the firm news arrived of the great discovery of diamonds among the Ural Mountains </s>
<s> The first intimation was received through the Central News Agency in the form of the following telegram:-- "Moscow, _August_ 22.--It is reported from Tobolsk that an important discovery of diamond fields has been made amongst the spurs of the Ural Mountains, at a point not very far from that city </s>
<s> They are said to have been found by an English geologist, who has exhibited many magnificent gems in proof of his assertion </s>
<s> These stones have been examined at Tobolsk, and are pronounced to be equal, if not superior, in quality to any found elsewhere </s>
<s> A company has been already formed for the purpose of purchasing the land and working the mines" </s>
<s> Some days afterwards there came a Reuter's telegram giving fuller details </s>
<s> "With regard to the diamond fields near Tobolsk," it said, "there is every reason to believe that they are of great, and possibly unsurpassed, wealth </s>
<s> There is no question now as to their authenticity, since their discoverer proves to be an English gentleman of high character, and his story is corroborated by villagers from this district who have dug up stones for themselves </s>
<s> The Government contemplate buying out the company and taking over the mines, which might be profitably worked by the forced labour of political prisoners on a system similar to that adopted in the salt mines of Siberia </s>
<s> The discovery is universally regarded as one which has materially increased the internal resources of the country, and there is some talk of the presentation of a substantial testimonial to the energetic and scientific traveller to whom it is due" </s>
<s> Within a week or ten days of the receipt of these telegrams in London there came letters from the Russian correspondents of the various journals giving fuller details upon a subject of so much general interest </s>
<s> The _Times_ directed attention to the matter in a leader </s>
<s> "It appears," remarked the great paper, "that a most important addition has been made to the mineral wealth of the Russian Empire </s>
<s> The silver mines of Siberia and the petroleum wells of the Caucasus are to be outrivalled by the new diamond fields of the Ural Mountains </s>
<s> For untold thousands of years these precious fragments of crystallized carbon have been lying unheeded among the gloomy gorges waiting for the hand of man to pick them out </s>
<s> It has fallen to the lot of one of our countrymen to point out to the Russian nation the great wealth which lay untouched and unsuspected in the heart of their realm </s>
<s> The story is a romantic one </s>
<s> It appears that a Mr Langworthy, a wealthy English gentleman of good extraction, had, in the course of his travels in Russia, continued his journey as far as the great mountain barrier which separates Europe from Asia </s>
<s> Being fond of sport, he was wandering in search of game down one of the Ural valleys, when his attention was attracted by the thick gravel, which was piled up along the track of a dried-up water-course </s>
<s> The appearance and situation of this gravel reminded him forcibly of the South African diamond fields, and so strong was the impression that he at once laid down his gun and proceeded to rake the gravel over and to examine it </s>
<s> His search was rewarded by the discovery of several stones, which he conveyed home with him, and which proved, after being cleaned, to be gems of the first water </s>
<s> Elated at this success, he returned to the spot next day with a spade, and succeeded in obtaining many other specimens, and in convincing himself that the deposit stretched up and down for a long distance on both sides of the torrent </s>
<s> Having satisfied himself upon this point, our compatriot made his way to Tobolsk, where he exhibited his prizes to several of the richest merchants, and proceeded to form a company for the working of the new fields </s>
<s> He was so successful in this that the shares are already far above par, and our correspondent writes that there has been a rush of capitalists, all eager to invest their money in so promising a venture </s>
<s> It is expected that within a few months the necessary plant will have been erected and the concern be in working order" </s>
<s> The _Daily Telegraph_ treated the matter from a jocose and historical point of view </s>
<s> "It has long been a puzzle to antiquaries and geologists," it remarked, "as to where those jewels which Solomon brought from the East were originally obtained </s>
<s> There has been much speculation, too, regarding the source of those less apocryphal gems which sparkled in the regalia of the Indian monarchs and adorned the palaces of Delhi and Benares </s>
<s> As a nation we have a personal interest in the question, since the largest and most magnificent of these stones is now in the possession of our most gracious Queen </s>
<s> Mr Langworthy has thrown a light upon this obscure subject </s>
<s> According to this gentleman's researches these treasures were unearthed amidst that dark and gloomy range of mountains which Providence has interposed between a nascent civilization and a continent of barbarians </s>
<s> Nor is Mr Langworthy's opinion founded upon theory alone </s>
<s> He lends point to his arguments by presenting to the greedy eyes of the merchants of Tobolsk a bag filled with valuable diamonds, each and every one of which he professes to have discovered in these barren inhospitable valleys </s>
<s> This tweed-suited English tourist, descending like some good spirit among these dreamy Muscovites, points out to them the untold wealth which has lain for so many centuries at their feet, and with the characteristic energy of his race shows them at the same time how to turn the discovery to commercial advantage </s>
<s> If the deposit prove to be as extensive as is supposed, it is possible that our descendants may wear cut diamonds in their eye-glasses, should such accessories be necessary, and marvel at the ignorance of those primitive days when a metamorphosed piece of coal was regarded as the most valuable product of nature" </s>
<s> The ordinary British paterfamilias, glancing over his morning paper, bestowed probably but few passing thoughts on the incident, but among business men and in the City its significance was at once understood </s>
<s> Not only did it create the deepest consternation amongst all who were connected with the diamond industry, but it reacted upon every other branch of South African commerce </s>
<s> It was the chief subject of conversation upon the Stock Exchange, and many were the surmises as to what the effect of the news would be at the fields </s>
<s> Fugger, the father of the diamond industry, was standing discussing the question, when a little rosy-faced Jew, named Goldschmidt, came bustling up to him </s>

<s> "Misther Fugger," he cried, "you're shust the man I want to see </s>
<s> My Gott, vot is to become of us all </s>
<s> Vot is to become of de diamond trade ven one can pick them up like cockles on the sea shore" </s>
<s> "We must wait for details," the great financier said phlegmatically </s>
<s> His fortune was so enormous that it mattered little to him whether the report was true or false </s>
<s> "Details </s>
<s> It is nothing but details," cried the little Jew </s>
<s> "The papers is full of them </s>
<s> I vish to the Lord that that Langworthy had proke his neck in the Ural Mountains before he got up to any such games </s>

<s> Nobody that's any good would ever go to the Ural Mountains at all" </s>

<s> "Von't it, by Joves </s>
<s> Why, man, I've got over a hundred shtones on my hands now </s>
<s> Vat am I going to do vid 'em" </s>

<s> CHAPTER XX </s>
<s> MR </s>
<s> HECTOR O'FLAHERTY FINDS SOMETHING IN THE PAPER </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone had taken up his quarters in two private rooms at the _Central Hotel_, Kimberley, and had already gained a considerable reputation in the town by the engaging "abandon" of his manners, and by the munificent style in which he entertained the more prominent citizens of the little capital </s>

<s> At quarter-past one Hebron was up and aghast at the news </s>
<s> At three in the morning a mounted messenger galloped into Bluejacket, and before daybreak a digger committee was sitting at Delporte's Hope discussing the situation </s>
<s> So during that eventful night down the whole long line of the Vaal River there was ruin and heartburning and dismay, while five thousand miles away an old gentleman was sleeping calmly and dreamlessly in his comfortable bed, from whose busy brain had emanated all this misery and misfortune </s>
<s> Perhaps the said old gentleman might have slumbered a little less profoundly could he have seen the sight which met his son's eyes on the following morning </s>
<s> Ezra had passed the night at Dutoitspan, in the hut of a hospitable miner </s>
<s> Having risen in the morning, he was dressing himself in a leisurely, methodical fashion, when his host, who had been inhaling the morning breeze, thrust his head through the window </s>
<s> "Come out here, Mr Girdlestone," he cried </s>
<s> "There's some fun on </s>
<s> One of the boys is dead drunk, and they are carrying him in" </s>
<s> Ezra pulled on his coat and ran out </s>
<s> A little group of miners were walking slowly up the main street </s>
<s> He and his host were waiting for the procession to pass them with several jocose remarks appropriate to the occasion ready upon their lips, when their eyes fell upon a horrible splotchy red track which marked the road the party had taken </s>
<s> They both ran forward with exclamations and inquiries </s>
<s> "It's Jim Stewart," said one of the bearers </s>
<s> "Him that they used to call Unlucky Jim" </s>
<s> "What's up with him" </s>
<s> "He has shot himself through the head </s>
<s> Where d'ye think we found him </s>
<s> Slap in the middle o' his own claim, with his fingers dug into the gravel, as dead as a herring" </s>
<s> "He's a bad plucked 'un to knock under like that," Ezra's companion remarked </s>
<s> "Yes," said the croupier of the saloon gambling table </s>
<s> "If he'd waited for another deal he might have held every trump </s>
<s> He was always a soft chap, was Jim, and he was saying last night as how this spoiled the last chance he was ever like to have of seeing his wife and childer in England </s>
<s> He's blowed a fine clean hole in himself </s>
<s> Would you like to see it, Mr Girdlestone" </s>
<s> The fellow was about to remove the blood-stained handkerchief which covered the dead man's face, but Ezra recoiled in horror </s>
<s> "Mr Girdlestone looks faint like," some one observed </s>
<s> "Yes," said Ezra, who was white to his very lips </s>
<s> "This has upset me rather </s>
<s> I'll have a drop of brandy" </s>
<s> As he walked back to the hut, he wondered inwardly whether the incident would have discomposed his father </s>
<s> "I suppose he would call it part of our commercial finesse," he said bitterly to himself </s>
<s> "However, we have put our hands to the plough, and we must not let homicide stop us" </s>
<s> So saying, he steadied his nerves with a draught of brandy, and prepared for the labours of the day </s>
<s> CHAPTER XXI </s>
<s> AN UNEXPECTED BLOW </s>
<s> The crisis at the African fields was even more acute than had been anticipated by the conspirators </s>
<s> Nothing approaching to it had ever been known in South Africa before </s>
<s> Diamonds went steadily down in value until they were selling at a price which no dealer would have believed possible, and the sale of claims reached such a climax that men were glad to get rid of them for the mere price of the plant and machinery erected at them </s>
<s> The offices of the various dealers at Kimberley were besieged night and day by an importunate crowd of miners, who were willing to sell at any price in order to save something from the general ruin which they imagined was about to come upon the industry </s>
<s> Some, more long-headed or more desperate than their neighbours, continued to work their claims and to keep the stones which they found until prices might be better </s>
<s> As fresh mails came from the Cape, however, each confirming and amplifying the ominous news, these independent workers grew fewer and more faint-hearted, for their boys had to be paid each week, and where was the money to come from with which to pay them </s>
<s> The dealers, too, began to take the alarm, and the most tempting offers would hardly induce them to give hard cash in exchange for stones which might prove to be a drug in the market </s>
<s> Everywhere there was misery and stagnation </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone was not slow to take advantage of this state of things, but he was too cunning to do so in a manner which might call attention to himself or his movements </s>
<s> In his wanderings he had come across an outcast named Farintosh, a man who had once been a clergyman and a master of arts of Trinity College, Dublin, but who was now a broken-down gambler with a slender purse and a still more slender conscience </s>
<s> He still retained a plausible manner and an engaging address, and these qualities first recommended him to the notice of the young merchant </s>
<s> A couple of days after the receipt of the news from Europe, Ezra sent for this fellow and sat with him for some time on the verandah of the hotel, talking over the situation </s>
<s> "You see, Farintosh," he remarked, "it might be a false alarm, might it not" </s>
<s> The ex-clergyman nodded </s>
<s> He was a man of few words </s>
<s> "If it should be, it would be an excellent thing for those who buy now" </s>
<s> Farintosh nodded once again </s>
<s> "Of course," Ezra continued, "it looks as if the thing was beyond all doubt </s>
<s> My experience has taught me, however, that there is nothing so uncertain as a certainty </s>
<s> That's what makes me think of speculating over this </s>
<s> If I lose it won't hurt me much, and I might win </s>
<s> I came out here more for the sake of seeing a little of the world than anything else, but now that this has turned up I'll have a shy at it" </s>
<s> "Quite so," said Farintosh, rubbing his hands </s>
<s> "You see," Ezra continued, lighting a cheroot, "I have the name here of having a long purse and of knowing which way the wind blows </s>
<s> If I were to be seen buying others would follow my lead, and prices would soon be as high as ever </s>
<s> Now, what I purpose is to work through you, d'ye see </s>
<s> You can take out a licence and buy in stones on the quiet without attracting much attention </s>
<s> Beat them down as low as you can, and give this hotel as your address </s>
<s> When they call here they shall be paid, which is better than having you carrying the money round with you" </s>
<s> The clergyman scowled as though he thought it was anything but better </s>
<s> He did not make any remark, however </s>
<s> "You can get one or two fellows to help you," said Ezra </s>
<s> "I'll pay for their licences </s>
<s> I can't expect you to work all the camps yourself </s>
<s> Of course, if you offer more for a stone than I care to give, that's your look out, but if you do your work well you shall not be the loser </s>
<s> You shall have a percentage on business done and a weekly salary as well" </s>
<s> "How much money do you care to invest" </s>
<s> asked Farintosh </s>
<s> "I'm not particular," Ezra answered </s>
<s> "If I do a thing I like to do it well </s>
<s> I'll go the length of thirty thousand pounds" </s>
<s> Farintosh was so astonished at the magnitude of the sum that he sank back in his chair in bewilderment </s>
<s> "Why, sir," he said, "I think just at present you could buy the country for that" </s>
<s> Ezra laughed </s>
<s> "We'll make it go as far as we can," he said </s>
<s> "Of course you may buy claims as well as stones" </s>
<s> "And I have carte blanche to that amount" </s>
<s> "Certainly" </s>
<s> "All right, I'll begin this evening," said the ex-parson; and picking up his slouched hat, which he still wore somewhat broader in the brim than his comrades, in deference to old associations, he departed upon his mission </s>
<s> Farintosh was a clever man and soon chose two active subordinates </s>
<s> These were a navvy, named Burt, and Williams, a young Welshman, who had disappeared from home behind a cloud of forged cheques, and having changed his name had made a fresh start in life to the south of the equator </s>
<s> These three worked day and night buying in stones from the more needy and impecunious miners, to whom ready money was a matter of absolute necessity </s>
<s> Farintosh bought in the stock, too, of several small dealers whose nerves had been shaken by the panic </s>
<s> In this way bag after bag was filled with diamonds by Ezra, while he himself was to all appearances doing nothing but smoking cigars and sipping brandy-and-water in front of the _Central Hotel_ </s>
<s> He was becoming somewhat uneasy in his mind as to how long the delusion would be kept up, or how soon news might come from the Cape that the Ural find had been examined into and had proved to be a myth </s>
<s> In any case, he thought that he would be free from suspicion </s>
<s> Still, it might be as well for him by that time to be upon his homeward journey, for he knew that if by any chance the true facts leaked out there would be no hope of mercy from the furious diggers </s>
<s> Hence he incited Farintosh to greater speed, and that worthy divine with his two agents worked so energetically that in less than a week there was little left of five and thirty thousand pounds </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone had shown his power of reading character when he chose the ex-clergyman as his subordinate </s>
<s> It is possible, however, that the young man's judgment had been inferior to his powers of observation </s>
<s> A clever man as a trusty ally is a valuable article, but when the said cleverness may be turned against his employer the advantage becomes a questionable one </s>
<s> It was perfectly evident to Farintosh that though a stray capitalist might risk a thousand pounds or so on a speculation of this sort, Rothschild himself would hardly care to invest such a sum as had passed through his hands without having some ground on which to go </s>
<s> Having formed this conclusion, and having also turned over in his mind the remarkable coincidence that the news of this discovery in Russia should follow so very rapidly upon the visit of the junior partner of the House of Girdlestone, the astute clergyman began to have some dim perception of the truth </s>
<s> Hence he brooded a good deal as he went about his work, and cogitated deeply in a manner which was once again distinctly undesirable in so very intelligent a subordinate </s>
<s> These broodings and cogitations culminated in a meeting, which was held by him with his two sub-agents in the private parlour of the Digger's Retreat </s>
<s> It was a low-roofed, smoke-stained room, with a profusion of spittoons scattered over it, which, to judge by the condition of the floor, the patrons of the establishment had taken some pains to avoid </s>
<s> Round a solid, old-fashioned table in the centre of this apartment sat Ezra's staff of assistants, the parson thoughtful but self-satisfied, the others sullen and inquisitive </s>
<s> Farintosh had convened the meeting, and his comrades had an idea that there was something in the wind </s>
<s> They applied themselves steadily, therefore, to the bottle of Hollands upon the table, and waited for him to speak </s>
<s> "Well," the ex-clergyman said at last, "the game is nearly over, and we'll not be wanted any more </s>
<s> Girdlestone's off to England in a day or two" </s>
<s> Burt and Williams groaned sympathetically </s>
<s> Work was scarce in the diggings during the crisis, and their agencies had been paying them well </s>
<s> "Yes, he's off," Farintosh went on, glancing keenly at his companions, "and he takes with him five and thirty thousand pounds worth of diamonds that we bought for him </s>
<s> Poor devils like us, Burt, have to do the work, and then are thrown aside as you would throw your pick aside when you are done with it </s>
<s> When he sells out in London and makes his pile, it won't much matter to him that the three men who helped him are starving in Griqualand" </s>
<s> "Won't he give us somethin' at partin'" </s>
<s> asked Burt, the navvy </s>
<s> He was a savage-looking, hairy man, with a brick-coloured face and over-hanging eyebrows </s>
<s> "Won't he give us nothing to remembrance him by" </s>
<s> "Give you something" </s>
<s> Farintosh said with a sneer </s>
<s> "Why, man, he says you are too well paid already" </s>
<s> "Does he, though" </s>
<s> cried the navvy, flushing even redder than nature had made him </s>
<s> "Is that the way he speaks after we makes him </s>
<s> It ain't on the square </s>
<s> I likes to see things honest an' above board betwixt man an' man, and this pitchin' of them as has helped ye over ain't that" </s>
<s> Farintosh lowered his voice and bent further over the table </s>
<s> His companions involuntarily imitated his movement, until the three cunning, cruel faces were looking closely into one another's eyes </s>
<s> "Nobody knows that he holds those stones," said Farintosh </s>
<s> "He's too smart to let it out to any one but ourselves" </s>
<s> "Where does he keep 'em" </s>
<s> asked the Welshman </s>
<s> "In a safe in his room" </s>
<s> "Where is the key" </s>
<s> "On his watch-chain" </s>
<s> "Could we get an impression" </s>
<s> "I have one" </s>
<s> "Then I can make one," cried Williams triumphantly </s>
<s> "It's done," said Farintosh, taking a small key from his pocket </s>
<s> "This is a duplicate, and will open the safe </s>
<s> I took the moulding from his key while I was speaking to him" </s>
<s> The navvy laughed hoarsely </s>
<s> "If that don't lick creation for smartness" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "And how are we to get to this safe </s>
<s> It would serve him right if we collar the lot </s>
<s> It'll teach him that if he ain't honest by nature he's got to be when he deals with the like of us </s>
<s> I like straightness, and by the Lord I'll have it" </s>
<s> He brought his great fist down upon the table to emphasize this commendable sentiment </s>
<s> "It's not an easy matter," Farintosh said thoughtfully </s>
<s> "When he goes out he locks his door, and there's no getting in at the window </s>
<s> There's only one chance for us that I can see </s>
<s> His room is a bit cut off from the rest of the hotel </s>
<s> There's a gallery of twenty feet or more that leads to it </s>
<s> Now, I was thinking that if the three of us were to visit him some evening, just to wish him luck on his journey, as it were, and if, while we were in the room something sudden was to happen which would knock him silly for a minute or two, we might walk off with the stones and be clean gone before he could raise an alarm" </s>
<s> "And what would knock him silly" </s>

<s> He grasped the youth's white wrist and squeezed it in his iron grip until he writhed with the pain </s>
<s> "Oh, I'm with you, heart and soul," he cried </s>
<s> "I'm sure what you and Mr Farintosh advise must be for the best" </s>

<s> "We can get it over by nine, and we will have the night for our escape </s>
<s> I'll have the horses ready, and it will be strange if we don't get such a start as will puzzle them" </s>
<s> So, having arranged all the details of their little plan, these three gentlemen departed in different directions--Farintosh to the _Central Hotel_, to give Ezra his evening report, and the others to the mining-camps, which were the scene of their labours </s>
<s> The meeting just described took place upon a Tuesday, early in November </s>
<s> On the Saturday Ezra Girdlestone had fully made up his mind to turn his back upon the diggings and begin his homeward journey </s>
<s> He was pining for the pleasures of his old London life, and was weary of the monotonous expanse of the South African veldt </s>
<s> His task was done, too, and it would be well for him to be at a distance before the diggers discovered the manner in which they had been hoaxed </s>
<s> He began to pack his boxes, therefore, and to make every preparation for his departure </s>
<s> He was busily engaged in this employment upon the Wednesday evening when there was a tap at the door and Farintosh walked in, accompanied by Burt and Williams </s>
<s> Girdlestone glanced up at them, and greeted them briefly </s>
<s> He was not surprised at their visit, for they had come together several times before to report progress or make arrangements </s>
<s> Farintosh bowed as he entered the room, Burt nodded, and Williams rubbed his hands together and looked amiably bilious </s>
<s> "We looked in, Mr Girdlestone," Farintosh began, "to learn if you had any commands for us" </s>
<s> "I told you before that I had not," Ezra said curtly </s>
<s> "I am going on Saturday </s>
<s> I have made a mistake in speculating on those diamonds </s>
<s> Prices are sinking lower and lower" </s>
<s> "I am sorry to hear that," said Farintosh sympathetically </s>
<s> "Maybe the market will take a turn" </s>
<s> "Let us hope so," the merchant answered </s>
<s> "It doesn't look like it" </s>

<s> "We have done our work all right, haven't we" </s>
<s> "I have nothing to complain of," Ezra said coldly </s>
<s> "Well then, guv'nor, you surely ain't going away without leaving us nothing to remembrance you with, seeing that we've stood by you and never gone back on you" </s>
<s> "You have been paid every week for what you have done," the young man said </s>

<s> cried the navvy angrily </s>
<s> "No, I won't; and I'll tell you what it is, Burt, big as you are, if you dare to raise your voice in my presence I'll give you the soundest hiding that ever you had in your life" </s>

<s> The guilty trio stole out of the room, bearing their plunder with them, and walked down the passage of the hotel unmolested and unharmed </s>
<s> The moon, as it rose over the veldt that night, shone on three horsemen spurring it along the Capetown road as though their very lives depended upon their speed </s>
<s> Its calm, clear rays streamed over the silent roofs of Kimberley and in through a particular window of the _Central Hotel_, throwing silvery patches upon the carpet, and casting strange shadows from the figure which lay as it had fallen, huddled in an ungainly heap upon the floor </s>
<s> CHAPTER XXII </s>
<s> ROBBERS AND ROBBED </s>
<s> It might perhaps have been as well for the curtailing of this narrative, and for the interests of the world at large if the blow dealt by the sturdy right arm of the navvy had cut short once for all the career of the junior African merchant </s>
<s> Ezra, however, was endowed with a rare vitality, which enabled him not only to shake off the effects of his mishap, but to do so in an extraordinarily short space of time </s>
<s> There was a groan from the prostrate figure, then a feeble movement, then another and a louder groan, and then an oath </s>
<s> Gradually raising himself upon his elbow, he looked around him in a bewildered way, with his other hand pressed to the wound at the back of his head, from which a few narrow little rivulets of blood were still meandering </s>
<s> His glance wandered vaguely over the table and the chairs and the walls, until it rested upon the safe </s>
<s> He could see in the moonlight that it was open, and empty </s>
<s> In a moment the whole circumstances of the case came back to him, and he staggered to the door with a hoarse cry of rage and of despair </s>
<s> Whatever Ezra's faults may have been, irresolution or want of courage were not among them </s>
<s> In a moment he grasped the situation, and realized that it was absolutely essential that he should act, and at once </s>
<s> The stones must be recovered, or utter and irretrievable ruin stared him in the face </s>
<s> At his cries the landlord and several attendants, white and black, came rushing into the room </s>
<s> "I've been robbed and assaulted," Ezra said, steadying himself against the mantelpiece, for he was still weak and giddy </s>
<s> "Don't all start cackling, but do what I ask you </s>
<s> Light the lamp" </s>
<s> The lamp was lit, and there was a murmur from the little knot of employees, reinforced by some late loungers at the bar, as they saw the disordered room and the great crimson patch upon the carpet </s>
<s> "The thieves called at nine," said Ezra, talking rapidly, but collectedly </s>
<s> "Their names were Farintosh, Burt, and Williams </s>
<s> We talked for, some little time, so they probably did not leave the house before a quarter past at the soonest </s>
<s> It is now half-past ten, so they have no very great start </s>
<s> You, Jamieson, and you, Van Muller, run out and find if three men have been seen getting away </s>
<s> Perhaps they took a buggy </s>
<s> Go up and down, and ask all you see </s>
<s> You, Jones, go as hard as you can to Inspector Ainslie </s>
<s> Tell him there has been robbery and attempted murder, and say that I want half a dozen of his best mounted men--not his best men, you understand, but his best horses </s>
<s> I shall see that he is no loser if he is smart </s>
<s> Where's my servant Pete </s>
<s> Pete, you dog, get my horse saddled and bring her round </s>
<s> She ought to be able to catch anything in Griqualand" </s>
<s> As Ezra gave his orders the men hurried off in different directions to carry them out </s>
<s> He himself commenced to arrange his dress, and tied a handkerchief tightly round his head </s>
<s> "Surely you are not going, sir" </s>
<s> the landlord said, "You are not fit" </s>
<s> "Fit or not, I am going," Ezra said resolutely </s>
<s> "If I have to be strapped to my horse I'll go </s>
<s> Send me up some brandy </s>
<s> Put some in a flask, too </s>
<s> I may feel faint before I get back" </s>
<s> A great concourse of people had assembled by this time, attracted by the report of the robbery </s>
<s> The whole square in front of the hotel was crowded with diggers and store-keepers and innumerable Kaffirs, all pressing up to the portico in the hope of hearing some fresh details </s>
<s> Mr Hector O'Flaherty, over the way, was already busy setting up his type in preparation for a special edition, in which the _Vaal River Advertiser_ should give its version of the affair </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXIII </s>
<s> A MOMENTOUS RESOLUTION </s>
<s> During the months which Ezra Girdlestone had spent in Africa the affairs of the firm in Fenchurch Street had been exceedingly prosperous </s>
<s> Trade upon the coast had been brisker than usual, and three of the company's ships had come in at short intervals with excellent cargoes </s>
<s> Among these was the _Black Eagle_ which, to the astonishment of Captain Hamilton Miggs and the disgust of his employer, had weathered a severe gale in the Channel, and had arrived safe and sound once more </s>
<s> This run of luck, supplemented by the business capacity of the old merchant and the indomitable energy of young Dimsdale, made the concern look so flourishing that the former felt more than ever convinced that if he could but stave off the immediate danger things would soon right themselves </s>
<s> Hence he read with delight the letters from Africa, in which his son narrated the success of the conspiracy and the manner in which the miners had been hoodwinked </s>
<s> The old man's figure grew straighter and his step more firm as the conviction grew upon him that the company would soon return once again to its former condition of affluence </s>
<s> It may be imagined, therefore, that when the rumours of a bona fide diamond find in the Orange Free State came to his ears John Girdlestone was much agitated and distressed </s>
<s> On the same day that he saw the announcement in the papers he received a letter from his son announcing the failure of their enterprise </s>
<s> After narrating the robbery, the pursuit, the death of Farintosh, and the announcement of the new discovery, it gave an account of his subsequent movements </s>
<s> "There was no doubt about the truth of the scoundrel's words," he said, "for when we went to the nearest farm to get some food and have the sergeant's wound dressed we found that every one was talking about it </s>
<s> There was a chap there who had just come from the State and knew all about it </s>
<s> After hearing the details from him I saw that there was no doubt of the genuineness of the thing </s>
<s> "The police rode back to Jacobsdal with Williams, and I promised to come after them; but when I came to think it over it didn't seem good enough </s>
<s> The fact of my having so many diamonds would set every tongue wagging, and, again, the sergeant had heard what Farintosh said to me, so it was very possible that I might have the whole district about my ears </s>
<s> As it was, I had the stones and all my money in the bag </s>
<s> I wrote back to the hotel, therefore, telling the landlord to send on my traps to Cape Town by mail, and promising to settle my bill with him when I received them </s>
<s> I then bought a horse and came straight south </s>
<s> I shall take the first steamer and be with you within a few days of your receiving this </s>
<s> "As to our speculation, it is, of course, all up </s>
<s> Even when the Russian business proves to be a hoax, the price of stones will remain very low on account of these new fields </s>
<s> It is possible that we may sell our lot at some small profit but it won't be the royal road to a fortune that you prophesied, nor will it help the firm out of the rut into which you have shoved it </s>
<s> My only regret in leaving Africa like this is that that vermin Williams will have no one to prosecute him </s>
<s> My head is almost well now" </s>
<s> This letter was a rude shock to the African merchant </s>
<s> Within a week of the receipt of it his son Ezra, gloomy and travel-stained, walked into the sanctum at Fenchurch Street and confirmed all the evil tidings by word of mouth </s>
<s> The old man was of too tough a fibre to break down completely, but his bony hands closed convulsively upon the arms of the chair, and a cold perspiration broke out upon his wrinkled forehead as he listened to such details as his son vouchsafed to afford him </s>
<s> "You have your stones all safe, though" </s>
<s> he stammered out at last </s>
<s> "They are in my box, at home," said Ezra, gloomy and morose, leaning against the white marble mantelpiece </s>
<s> "The Lord knows what they are worth </s>
<s> We'll be lucky if we clear as much as they cost and a margin for my expenses and Langworthy's </s>
<s> A broken head is all that I have got from your fine scheme" </s>
<s> "Who could foresee such a thing" </s>
<s> the old man said plaintively </s>
<s> He might have added Major Clutterbuck's thousand pounds as another item to be cleared, but he thought it as well to keep silent upon the point </s>
<s> "Any fool could foresee the possibility of it," quoth Ezra brusquely </s>
<s> "The fall in prices is sure to be permanent, then" </s>
<s> the old man asked </s>
<s> "It will last for some years, any way," Ezra answered </s>
<s> "The Jagersfontein gravel is very rich, and there seems to be plenty of it" </s>
<s> "And within a few months we must repay both capital and interest </s>
<s> We are ruined" </s>
<s> The old merchant spoke in a broken voice, and his head sank upon his breast </s>
<s> "When that day comes," he continued, "the firm which has been for thirty years above reproach, and a model to the whole City, will be proclaimed as a bankrupt concern </s>
<s> Worse still, it will be shown to have been kept afloat for years by means which will be deemed fraudulent </s>

<s> If it had ruined itself it would be easier to bear it, but it is sacrificed to outside speculations--my wretched, wretched speculations </s>

<s> He touched the bell, and Gilray answered the summons </s>
<s> "Listen to this, Ezra </s>

<s> "But Girdlestone becomes a sleeping partner," said Ezra </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXIV </s>
<s> A DANGEROUS PROMISE </s>
<s> During Ezra Girdlestone's absence in Africa our heroine's life had been even less eventful than of old </s>
<s> There was a consistency about the merchant's establishment which was characteristic of the man </s>
<s> The house itself was austere and gloomy, and every separate room, in spite of profuse expenditure and gorgeous furniture, had the same air of discomfort </s>
<s> The servants too, were, with one single exception, from the hard-visaged housekeeper to the Calvinistic footman, a depressing and melancholy race </s>
<s> The only departure from this general rule was Kate's own maid, Rebecca Taylforth, a loudly-dressed, dark-eyed, coarse-voiced young woman, who raised up her voice and wept when Ezra departed for Africa </s>
<s> This damsel's presence was most disagreeable to Kate, and, indeed, to John Girdlestone also, who only retained her on account of his son's strong views upon the subject, and out of fear of an explosion which might wreck all his plans </s>
<s> The old merchant was Kate's only companion during this period, and their conversation was usually limited to a conventional inquiry at breakfast time as to each other's health </s>
<s> On his return from the City in the evening Girdlestone was always in a moody humour, and would eat his dinner hastily and in silence </s>
<s> After dinner he was in the habit of reading methodically the various financial articles in the day's papers, which would occupy him until bedtime </s>
<s> Occasionally his companion would read these aloud to him, and such was the monotony of her uneventful life that she found herself becoming insensibly interested in the fluctuations of Grand Trunk scrip or Ohio and Delaware shares </s>
<s> The papers once exhausted, a bell was rung to summon the domestics, and when all were assembled the merchant, in a hard metallic voice, read through the lesson for the day and the evening prayers </s>
<s> On grand occasions he supplemented this by a short address, in the course of which he would pelt his frightened audience with hard jagged texts until he had reduced them to a fitting state of spiritual misery </s>
<s> No wonder that, under the influence of such an existence, the roses began to fade from his ward's cheeks, and her youthful heart to grow sad and heavy </s>
<s> One daily tonic there was, however, which never deserted her </s>
<s> Strictly as Girdlestone guarded her, and jealously as he fenced her off from the outer world, he was unable to prevent this one little ray of light penetrating her prison </s>
<s> With an eye to the future he had so placed her that it seemed to him to be impossible that any sympathy could reach her from the outside world </s>
<s> Visits and visitors were alike forbidden to her </s>
<s> On no consideration was she to venture out alone </s>
<s> In spite of all his precautions, however, love has many arts and wiles which defy all opposition, and which can outplot the deepest of plotters </s>
<s> Eccleston Square was by no means in a direct line between Kensington and the City, yet morning and evening, as sure as the clock pointed to half-past nine and to quarter to six, Tom would stride through the old-fashioned square and past the grim house, whose grimness was softened to his eyes through its association with the bright dream of his life </s>
<s> It was but the momentary glance of a sweet face at the upper window and a single wave of a white hand, but it sent him on with a fresh heart and courage, and it broke the dull monotony of her dreary life </s>
<s> Occasionally, as we have seen, he even managed to find his way into the interior of this ogre's castle, in which his fair princess was immured </s>
<s> John Girdlestone put an end to this by ordering that business messages should never under any circumstances be conveyed to his private residence </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXVI </s>
<s> BREAKING GROUND </s>
<s> In spite of John Girdlestone's temporary satisfaction and the stoical face which he presented to the world, it is probable that in the whole of London there was no more unhappy and heart-weary man </s>
<s> The long fight against impending misfortune had shattered his iron constitution and weakened him both in body and in mind </s>
<s> It was remarked upon 'Change how much he had aged of late, and moralists commented upon the vanity and inefficacy of the wealth which could not smooth the wrinkles from the great trader's haggard visage </s>
<s> He was surprised himself when he looked in the glass at the change which had come over him </s>
<s> "Never mind," he would say in his dogged heart a hundred times a day, "they can't beat me </s>
<s> Do what they will, they can't beat me" </s>
<s> This was the one thought which sustained and consoled him </s>
<s> The preservation of his commercial credit had become the aim and object of his life, to which there was nothing that he was not prepared to sacrifice </s>
<s> His cunningly devised speculation in diamonds had failed, but this failure had been due to an accident which could neither have been foreseen nor remedied </s>
<s> To carry out this scheme he had, as we have seen, been obliged to borrow money, which had now to be repaid </s>
<s> This he had managed to do, more or less completely, by the sale of the stones which Ezra had brought home, supplemented by the recent profits of the firm </s>
<s> There was still the original deficit to be faced, and John Girdlestone knew that though a settlement might be postponed from month to month, still the day must come, and come soon, when his debts must be met, or his inability to meet them become apparent to the whole world </s>
<s> Should Ezra be successful in his wooing and his ward's forty thousand pounds be thrown into the scale, the firm would shake itself clear from the load which oppressed it </s>

<s> The strangest of all the phenomena, however, presented by John Girdlestone at this period of his life was his own entire conviction of the righteousness of his actions </s>
<s> When every night and morning he sank upon his knees with his household and prayed for the success of the firm's undertakings, no qualms of conscience ever troubled him as to their intrinsic morality </s>
<s> On Sundays the grey head of the merchant in the first pew was as constant an object as was the pew itself, yet in that head no thought ever rose of the inconsistency of his religion and of his practice </s>
<s> For fifty years he had been persuading himself that he was a righteous man, and the conviction was now so firmly impressed upon his very soul that nothing could ever shake it </s>
<s> Ezra was wrong when he set this down as deliberate hypocrisy </s>
<s> Blind strength of will and self-conceit were at the bottom of his actions, but he would have been astonished and indignant had he been accused of simulating piety or of using it as a tool </s>
<s> To him the firm of Girdlestone was the very representation of religion in the commercial world, and as such must be upheld by every conceivable means </s>
<s> To his son this state of mind was unintelligible, and he simply gave his father credit for being a consummate and accomplished hypocrite, who found a mantle of piety a very convenient one under which to conceal his real character </s>
<s> He had himself inherited the old man's dogged pertinacity and commercial instincts, and was by nature unscrupulous and impatient of any obstacle placed in his way </s>
<s> He was now keenly alive to the fact that the existence of the firm depended upon the success of his suit, and he knew also how lucrative a concern the African business would prove were it set upon its legs again </s>

<s> His practical mind had already devised countless ways in which the profits might be increased </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXVII </s>
<s> MRS </s>
<s> SCULLY OF MORRISON'S </s>
<s> One day Major Tobias Clutterbuck was sitting at the window of his little room smoking his cigarette and sipping his glass of wine, as was his custom if times were reasonably good </s>
<s> While thus agreeably employed he chanced to look across the road and perceived a little fringe of dark hair, and a still darker eye, which surveyed him round the border of one of the curtains which flanked a window opposite </s>
<s> The gallant major was much interested in this apparition, and rose to make a closer inspection of it, but, alas </s>
<s> before he could focus it with his eye-glass it was gone </s>
<s> He bent his gaze resolutely in that direction for a long time, and smoked at least half a dozen cigarettes, besides finishing the bottle of wine; but although he thought he saw certain flittings and whiskings of garments in the dark background of the opposite room, he could not make out anything more definite </s>
<s> Next day the soldier was on the look-out at the same hour, and was rewarded by the appearance of two eyes, very mischievous and dangerous ones too, which were set in a buxom and by no means unprepossessing face </s>

<s> So much alarmed was she that she vanished behind the curtains and the major feared that he would see her no more </s>
<s> Fortunately, however, it became evident that the lady's alarm was not very overpowering, for within five minutes she was back at the window, where her eyes again fell upon the beaming face and jaunty figure of the major, who had posed himself in a striking attitude, which was somewhat marred by the fact that he was still enveloped in his purple dressing-gown </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXVIII </s>
<s> BACK IN BOHEMIA </s>
<s> Fortune had been smiling upon the Bohemians of late </s>
<s> Ever since the major's successful visit to Fenchurch Street he had been able to live in a state of luxury to which he had long been unaccustomed </s>
<s> His uncle, the earl, too, had condescended to think of his humble relative, and had made a small provision for him, which, with his other resources, removed all anxiety as to the future </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXIX </s>
<s> THE GREAT DANCE AT MORRISON'S </s>
<s> Never in the whole history of Morrison's boarding establishment had such festive preparations been known </s>
<s> The landlady herself had entered heart and soul into the business, and as all the boarders had received invitations for themselves and their friends, they co-operated in every possible manner to make the evening a success </s>
<s> The large drawing-room had been cleared and the floor waxed </s>
<s> This process left it in a very glassy and orthodox condition, as the cook discovered when, on bustling in, the back of her cranium came in violent contact with the boards, while her body described a half-circle with a velocity which completely eclipsed any subsequent feats of agility shown by the dancers in the evening </s>
<s> The saloon had been very tastefully laid out as a supper-room, and numerous other little chambers were thrown open and brightened up to serve as lounging places for those who were fatigued </s>
<s> In the parlour there were two card-tables, and every other convenience for any who preferred sedentary amusements </s>
<s> Altogether both Mrs Morrison and the boarders, in solemn conclave assembled, agreed that the thing looked very promising, and that it would be a credit to the establishment </s>
<s> The guests were as varied as the wines, though hardly as select </s>
<s> Mrs Scully's exuberant hospitality included, as already intimated, not only her own friends, but those of her fellow-boarders, so that from an early hour the rooms began to fill, and by nine o'clock there was hardly space for the dancers </s>
<s> Hansoms and growlers rattled up in a continuous stream and discharged their burdens </s>
<s> There was a carpet down from the kerb to the head of the lodging-house steps, "like r'yalty," as the cook expressed it, and the greengrocer's man in the hall looked so pompous and inflated in his gorgeous attire that his own cabbages would hardly have recognized him </s>
<s> His main defect as a footman was that he was somewhat hard of hearing, and had a marvellous faculty of misinterpreting whatever was said to him, which occasionally led to remarkable results </s>
<s> Thus, when he announced the sporting Captain Livingstone Tuck under the title of Captain Lives-on-his luck, it was felt that he was rather too near the truth to be pleasant </s>
<s> Indeed, the company had hardly recovered from the confusion produced by this small incident when the two Bohemians made their appearance </s>
<s> Mrs Scully, who was tastefully arrayed in black satin and lace, stood near the door of the drawing-room, and looked very charming and captivating as she fulfilled her duties as hostess </s>
<s> So thought the major as he approached her and shook her hand, with some well turned compliment upon his lips </s>
<s> "Let me inthroduce me friend, Herr von Baumser," he added </s>
<s> Mrs Scully smiled upon the German in a way that won his Teutonic heart </s>
<s> "You will find programmes over there," she explained </s>
<s> "I think the first is a round dance </s>

<s> She hurried away to greet a party of new arrivals, while the major and Baumser wandered off in search of partners </s>
<s> There was no want of spirit or of variety in the dancing at Morrison's </s>
<s> From Mr Snodder, the exciseman, who danced the original old-fashioned trois-temps, to young Bucklebury, of the Bank, who stationed himself immediately underneath the central chandelier, and spun rapidly round with his partner upon his own axis, like a couple of beetles impaled upon a single pin, every possible variation of the art of waltzing was to be observed </s>
<s> There was Mr Smith, of the Medical College, rotating round with Miss Clara Timms, their faces wearing that pained and anxious expression which the British countenance naturally assumes when dancing, giving the impression that the legs have suddenly burst forth in a festive mood, and have dragged the rest of the body into it very much against its will </s>
<s> There was the major too, who had succeeded in obtaining Mrs Scully as a partner, and was dancing as old soldiers can dance, threading his way through the crowded room with the ease begotten by the experience of a lifetime </s>
<s> Meanwhile Von Baumser, at the other end, was floundering about with a broad smile upon his face and an elderly lady tucked under his right arm, while he held her disengaged hand straight out at right angles, as if she had been a banjo </s>
<s> In short, the fun was fast and furious, and waltz followed polka and mazurka followed waltz with a rapidity which weeded out the weaker vessels among the dancers and tested the stamina of the musicians </s>
<s> Then there was the card-room, whither the Widow Scully and the major and many others of the elders repaired when they found the pace too fast for them </s>
<s> Very snug and comfortable it was, with its square tables, each with a fringe of chairs, and the clean shining cards spread out over their green baize surfaces </s>
<s> The major and his hostess played against Captain Livingstone Tuck and an old gentleman who came from Lambeth, with the result that the gallant captain and his partner rose up poorer and sadder men, which was rather a blow to the former, who reckoned upon clearing a little on such occasions, and had not expected to find himself opposed by such a past master of the art as the major </s>
<s> Then the veteran and another played the hostess and another lady, and the cunning old dog managed to lose in such a natural manner, and to pay up with such a good grace, and with so many pretty speeches and compliments, that the widow's partner was visibly impressed, a fact which, curiously enough, seemed to be anything but agreeable to the widow </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXX </s>
<s> AT THE "COCK AND COWSLIP" </s>
<s> Tom Dimsdale's duties were far from light </s>
<s> Not only was he expected to supervise the clerks' accounts and to treat with the wholesale dealers, but he was also supposed to spend a great part of his time in the docks, overlooking the loading of the outgoing ships and checking the cargo of the incoming ones </s>
<s> This latter portion of his work was welcome as taking him some hours a day from the close counting-house, and allowing him to get a sniff of the sea air--if, indeed, a sniff is to be had on the inland side of Woolwich </s>
<s> There was a pleasing life and bustle, too, in the broad, brown river, with its never-ending panorama of vessels of every size and shape which ebb and flow in the great artery of national life </s>
<s> So interesting was this liquid highway to Tom's practical mind, that he would often stand at the head of the wharf when his work was done and smoke a meditative pipe </s>
<s> It was a quiet spot, which had once been busy enough, but was now superseded by new quays and more convenient landing-places </s>
<s> All over it were scattered great rusty anchors, colossal iron chains, deserted melancholy boilers, and other debris which are found in such places, and which might seem to the fanciful to be the shells and skeletons of strange monsters washed up there by the tide </s>
<s> To whom do these things belong </s>
<s> Who has an interest in them </s>
<s> Of what use are they </s>
<s> It appeared to Tom sometimes as if the original owners and their heirs must have all died away, and left these grim relics behind them to any one who might have the charity to remove them </s>
<s> From this coign of vantage a long reach of the river was visible, and Tom sitting there would watch the fleets of passing vessels, and let his imagination wander away to the broad oceans which they had traversed, and the fair lands under bluer skies and warmer suns from which they had sailed </s>
<s> Here is a tiny steam-tug panting and toiling in front of a majestic three-master with her great black hulk towering out of the water and her masts shooting up until the topmast rigging looks like the delicate web of some Titanic spider </s>
<s> She is from Canton, with tea, and coffee, and spices, and all good things from the land of small feet and almond eyes </s>

<s> See how, as the darkness falls, a long row of yellow eyes glimmer out from her sides as the light streams through her countless portholes </s>

<s> A coasting brig has evidently had a wilder time still, for her main-topmast is cracked across, and her rigging is full of the little human mites who crawl about, and reef, and splice, and mend </s>
<s> An old acquaintance of ours was out in that same gale, and is even now making his way into the shelter of the Albert docks </s>
<s> This was none other than the redoubtable Captain Hamilton Miggs, whose ship will persistently keep afloat, to the astonishment of the gallant captain himself, and of every one else who knows anything of her sea-going qualities </s>
<s> Again and again she had been on the point of foundering; and again and again some change in the weather or the steady pumping of the crew had prevented her from fulfilling her destiny </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXIII </s>
<s> THE JOURNEY TO THE PRIORY </s>
<s> It was already dusk when John Girdlestone and his ward reached Waterloo Station </s>
<s> He gave orders to the guard that the luggage should be stamped, but took care that she should not hear the name of their destination </s>
<s> Hurrying her rapidly down the platform amid the confused heaps of luggage and currents of eager passengers, he pushed her into a first-class carriage, and sprang after her just as the bell rang and the wheels began to revolve </s>
<s> They were alone </s>
<s> Kate crouched up into the corner among the cushions, and wrapped her rug round her, for it was bitterly cold </s>
<s> The merchant pulled a note-book from his pocket and proceeded by the light of the lamp above him to add up columns of figures </s>
<s> He sat very upright in his seat, and appeared to be as absorbed in his work as though he were among his papers in Fenchurch Street </s>
<s> He neither glanced at his companion nor made any inquiry as to her comfort </s>
<s> As she sat opposite to him she could not keep her eyes from his hard angular face, every rugged feature of which was exaggerated by the flickering yellow light above him </s>
<s> Those deep-set eyes and sunken cheeks had been familiar to her for years </s>
<s> How was it that they now, for the first time, struck her as being terrible </s>
<s> Was it that new expression which had appeared upon them, that hard inexorable set about the mouth, which gave a more sinister character to his whole face </s>
<s> As she gazed at him an ineffable loathing and dread rose in her soul, and she could have shrieked out of pure terror </s>

<s> As she did so her guardian glanced over the top of the note-book with his piercing light grey eyes </s>
<s> "Don't get hysterical" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "You have given us trouble enough without that" </s>

<s> "You are right </s>
<s> I spoke too warmly </s>

<s> "You are becoming impertinent," he answered, and resumed his calculations in his note-book </s>
<s> Kate cowered back into her corner again, while the train thundered and screeched and rattled through the darkness </s>

<s> How long was she going for </s>
<s> What was she to do when there </s>
<s> On all these points she was absolutely ignorant </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXIV </s>
<s> THE MAN WITH THE CAMP-STOOL </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXV </s>
<s> A TALK ON THE LAWN </s>
<s> That same evening Rebecca came down from London </s>
<s> Her presence was a comfort to Kate, for though she had never liked or trusted the girl, yet the mere fact of having some one of her own age near her, gave her a sense of security and of companionship </s>
<s> Her room, too, had been altered for the better, and the maid was given the one next door, so that by knocking on the wall she could always communicate with her </s>
<s> This was an unspeakable consolation, for at night the old house was so full of the sudden crackings of warped timber and the scampering of rats that entire loneliness was unendurable </s>
<s> Apart from these uncanny sounds there were other circumstances which gave the Priory a sinister reputation </s>
<s> The very aspect of the building was enough to suggest weird impressions </s>
<s> Its high white walls were blotched with patches of mildew, and in some parts there were long greenish stains from roof to ground, like tear streaks on the crumbling plaster </s>
<s> Indoors there was a dank graveyard smell in the low corridors and narrow stair-cases </s>
<s> Floors and ceilings were equally worm-eaten and rotten </s>
<s> Broad flakes of plaster from the walls lay littered about in the passages </s>
<s> The wind, too, penetrated the building through many cracks and crannies, so that there was a constant sighing and soughing in the big dreary rooms, which had a most eerie and melancholy effect </s>
<s> Kate soon learned, however, that, besides these vague terrors, all predisposing the mind to alarm and exciting the imagination, there was a general belief that another more definite cause for fear existed in the old monastery </s>
<s> With cruel minuteness of detail her guardian had told her the legend which haunted those gloomy corridors </s>
<s> It appears that in olden times the Priory had been inhabited by Dominicans, and that in the course of years these monks had fallen away from their original state of sanctity </s>
<s> They preserved a name for piety among the country folk by their austere demeanour, but in secret, within the walls of their own monastery, they practised every sort of dissipation and crime </s>
<s> While the community was in this state of demoralization, each, from the abbot downwards, vying with the other in the number and enormity of their sins, there came a pious-minded youth from a neighbouring village, who begged that he might be permitted to join the order </s>
<s> He had been attracted, he said, by the fame of their sanctity </s>
<s> He was received amongst them, and at first was not admitted to their revels, but gradually, as his conscience was supposed to become more hardened, he was duly initiated into all their mysteries </s>
<s> Horrified by what he saw, the good youth concealed his indignation until he had mastered all the abominations of the establishment, and then, rising up on the altar steps, he denounced them in fiery, scathing words </s>
<s> He would leave them that night, he said, and he would tell his experiences through the length and breadth of the country </s>
<s> Incensed and alarmed, the friars held a hasty meeting, and then, seizing the young novice, they dragged him down the cellar steps and locked him up there </s>
<s> This same cellar had long been celebrated for the size and ferocity of the rats which inhabited it which were so fierce and strong that even during the day they had been known to attack those who entered </s>
<s> It is said that long into the weary hours of the night, the fearful shrieks and terrible struggles of the captive, as he fought with his innumerable assailants, resounded through the long corridors </s>
<s> "They do say that he walks about the house at times," Girdlestone said, in conclusion </s>
<s> "No one has ever been found who would live here very long since then </s>
<s> But, of course, such a strong-minded young woman as you, who cannot even obey your own guardian, would never be frightened by such a childish idea as that" </s>
<s> "I do not believe in ghosts, and I don't think I shall be frightened," Kate answered; but, for all that, the horrible story stuck in her mind, and added another to the many terrors which surrounded her </s>
<s> Mr Girdlestone's room was immediately above hers </s>
<s> On the second day of her imprisonment she went up on to this landing, for, having nothing to read save the Bible, and no materials for writing, she had little to do but to wander over the old house, and through the grounds </s>
<s> The door of Girdlestone's room was ajar, and she could not help observing as she passed that the apartment was most elegantly and comfortably furnished </s>
<s> So was the next room, the door of which was also open </s>
<s> The solid furniture and rich carpet contrasted strangely with her own bare, whitewashed chamber </s>
<s> All this pointed to the fact that her removal to the Priory had not been a sudden impulse on the part of the old merchant, but that he had planned and arranged every detail beforehand </s>
<s> Her refusal of Ezra was only the excuse for setting the machinery in motion </s>
<s> What was the object, then, and what was to be the end of this subtle scheming </s>
<s> That was the question which occurred to her every hour of the day, and every hour the answer seemed more grim and menacing </s>
<s> There was one link in the chain which was ever hidden from her </s>
<s> It had never occurred to the girl that her fortune could be of moment to the firm </s>
<s> She had been so accustomed to hear Ezra and his father talk glibly of millions, that she depreciated her own little capital and failed to realize how important it might be in a commercial crisis </s>
<s> Indeed, the possibility of such a crisis never entered her head, for one of her earliest impressions was hearing her father talk of the great resources of the firm and of its stability </s>
<s> That this firm was now in the direst straits, and that her money was absolutely essential to its existence, were things which never for one instant entered her thoughts </s>
<s> Yet that necessity was becoming more pressing every day </s>
<s> Ezra, in London, was doing all that indomitable energy and extraordinary business capacity could do to prolong the struggle </s>
<s> As debts became due, he would still stave off each creditor with such skill and plausibility as allayed every suspicion </s>
<s> Day by day, however, the work became more severe, and he felt that he was propping up an edifice which was so rotten that it must, sooner or later, come crumbling about his ears </s>
<s> When he came down to the Priory upon the Saturday, the young man's haggard and anxious face showed the severe ordeal which he had undergone </s>

<s> She heard the sound of the trap, however, and guessed who it was, even before his deep bass voice sounded in the room beneath </s>
<s> Looking out of her window a little later she saw him walking to and fro in the moonlight, talking earnestly to his father </s>
<s> It was a bitter night, and she wondered what they could have to talk about which might not be said beside the warm fire in the dining-room </s>
<s> They flickered up and down among the shadows for more than an hour, and then the girl heard the door slam, and shortly afterwards the heavy tread of the two men passed her chamber, and ascended to the rooms above </s>
<s> It was a momentous conversation which she had witnessed </s>
<s> In it Ezra had shown his father how impossible it was to keep up appearances, and how infallible was their ruin unless help came speedily </s>
<s> "I don't think any of them smell a rat," he said </s>
<s> "Mortimer and Johnson pressed for their bill in rather an ugly manner, but I talked them over completely </s>
<s> I took out my cheque-book </s>
<s> 'Look here, gentlemen,' said I, 'if you wish I shall write a cheque for the amount </s>
<s> If I do, it will be the last piece of business which we shall do together </s>
<s> A great house like ours can't afford to be disturbed in the routine of their business' </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXVI </s>
<s> THE INCIDENT OF THE CORRIDOR </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone hardly went through the formality of greeting Kate next morning when she came down to breakfast </s>
<s> He was evidently ill at ease, and turned away his eyes when she looked at him, though he glanced at her furtively from time to time </s>
<s> His father chatted with him upon City matters, but the young man's answers were brusque and monosyllabic </s>
<s> His sleep had been troubled and broken, for the conversation of the night before had obtruded unpleasantly on his dreams </s>
<s> Kate slipped away from them as soon as she could and, putting on her bonnet, went for a long walk through the grounds, partly for the sake of exercise, and partly in the hope of finding some egress </s>
<s> The one-eyed gate-keeper was at his post, and set up a hideous shout of laughter when he saw her; so she branched off among the trees to avoid him, and walked once more very carefully round the boundary wall </s>
<s> It was no easy matter to follow it continuously, for the briars and brambles grew in a confused tangle up to its very base </s>
<s> By perseverance, however, she succeeded in tracing every foot of it, and so satisfying herself finally that there was no diminution anywhere in its height, no break in its continuity, save the one small wooden door which was securely fastened </s>
<s> There was one spot, however, where a gleam of hope presented itself </s>
<s> At an angle of the wall there stood a deserted wooden shed, which had been used for the protection of gardeners' tools in the days when the grounds had been kept in better order </s>
<s> It was not buttressed up against the wall, but stood some eight or ten feet from it </s>
<s> Beside the shed was an empty barrel which had once been a water-butt </s>
<s> The girl managed to climb to the top of the barrel, and from this she was easily able to gain the sloping roof of the shed </s>
<s> Up this she clambered until she stood upon the summit, a considerable height above the ground </s>
<s> From it she was able to look down over the wall on to the country-road and the railway line which lay on the other side of it </s>
<s> True that an impassable chasm lay between her and the wall, but it would be surely possible for her to hail passers-by from here, and to persuade some of them to carry a letter to Bedsworth or to bring paper from there </s>
<s> Fresh hope gushed into her heart at the thought </s>
<s> It was not a very secure footing, for the planks of, which the shed was composed were worm-eaten and rotten </s>
<s> They cracked and crumbled beneath her feet, but what would she not dare to see a friendly human face </s>
<s> As she stood there a couple of country louts, young lads about sixteen, came strolling down the road, the one whistling and the other munching at a raw turnip </s>

<s> "Hey, Bill," he cried to his companion, "blowed if the mad wench bean't up on the shed over yander" </s>
<s> "So she be" </s>
<s> said the other eagerly </s>
<s> "Give me your turnip </s>
<s> Jimmy, an' I'll shy it at her" </s>
<s> "Noa, I'll shy it mysel'," said the gallant Jimmy; and at the word whizz came the half of a turnip within art inch of Kate's ear </s>

<s> shrieked the other savage </s>

<s> "Every man's hand is against me </s>
<s> I have only one true friend, and he is far away" </s>
<s> She went back to her room utterly disheartened and dispirited </s>

<s> "I trust," he said, "that you have read over the service </s>
<s> It is as well to do so when you cannot go to church" </s>
<s> "And why should you prevent me from going to church" </s>
<s> she asked </s>
<s> "Ah, my lady," he said with a sneer, "you are reaping what you have sown </s>
<s> You are tasting now, the bitter fruits of your disobedience </s>
