<s> CHAPTER XXXVII </s>
<s> A CHASE AND A BRAWL </s>
<s> It would be impossible to describe the suspense in which Tom Dimsdale lived during these weeks </s>
<s> In vain he tried in every manner to find some way of tracing the fugitives </s>
<s> He wandered aimlessly about London from one inquiry office to another, telling his story and appealing for assistance </s>
<s> He advertised in papers and cross-questioned every one who might know anything of the matter </s>
<s> There were none, however, who could help him or throw any light upon the mystery </s>
<s> No one at the office knew anything of the movements of the senior partner </s>

<s> He ate nothing and his sleep was much broken </s>

<s> Tom ran up to it </s>
<s> "Keep that red cab in sight," he said </s>
<s> "Whatever you do, don't let it get away from you" </s>

<s> Tom was afraid of losing sight of the two men in the crowd, so he elbowed his way through as quickly as he could, and got immediately behind them--so close that he could have touched them with his hand </s>
<s> They were approaching the booking-office, when Ezra glanced round and saw his rival standing behind him </s>
<s> He gave a bitter curse, and whispered something to his half-drunken companion </s>
<s> The latter turned, and with an inarticulate cry, like a wild beast, rushed at the young man and seized him by the throat with his brawny hands </s>
<s> It is one thing, however, to catch a man by the throat, and another to retain that grip, especially when your antagonist happens to be an International football player </s>
<s> To Tom this red-bearded rough, who charged him so furiously, was nothing more than the thousands of bull-headed forwards who had come upon him like thunder-bolts in the days of old </s>
<s> With the ease begotten by practice he circled his assailant with his long muscular arms, and gave a quick convulsive jerk in which every sinew of his body participated </s>

<s> All the cautions of his father and the exhortations of his mother were cast to the winds as he saw his enemy standing before him </s>

<s> They were well matched, for both were trained boxers and exceptionally powerful men </s>
<s> Ezra was perhaps the stronger, but Tom was in better condition </s>
<s> There was a short eager rally--blow and guard and counter so quick and hard that the eye could hardly follow it </s>

<s> "Where is he" </s>

<s> "He'll get away after all" </s>
<s> "Can't 'elp that," said the guardian of the peace phlegmatically </s>
<s> "A gen'elman like you ought to be ashamed </s>
<s> Keep quiet now </s>
<s> Would yer, then" </s>
<s> This last at some specially energetic effort on the part of the prisoner to recover his freedom </s>
<s> "They'll get away </s>
<s> I know they will" </s>
<s> Tom cried in despair, for both Ezra and his companion, who was none other than Burt, of African notoriety, had disappeared from his sight </s>
<s> His fears proved to be only too well founded, for when at last he succeeded in wresting himself from the constable's clutches he could find no trace of his enemies </s>

<s> He turned at last sadly and reluctantly away from the station, and walked across to Waterloo Bridge, brooding over all that had occurred, and cursing himself for his stupidity in allowing himself to be drawn into a vulgar brawl, when he might have attained his end so much better by quiet observation </s>
<s> It was some consolation, however, that he had had one fair crack at Ezra Girdlestone </s>
<s> He glanced down at his knuckles, which were raw and bleeding, with a mixture of satisfaction and disgust </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXIX </s>
<s> A GLEAM OF LIGHT </s>
<s> Kate Harston fled as quickly as she could through the wood, stumbling over the brambles and crashing through the briars, regardless of pain or scratches or anything else which could stand between her and the possibility of safety </s>
<s> She soon gained the shed and managed to mount on to the top of it by the aid of the barrel </s>
<s> Craning her neck, she could see the long dusty lane, with the bare withered hedges upon either side, and the dreary line of the railway embankment beyond </s>
<s> There was no pony-carriage in sight </s>
<s> She hardly expected that there would be, for she had taken a short cut, and the carriage would have to go some distance round </s>
<s> The road along which it was travelling ran at right angles to the one which she was now overlooking, and the chances were equal as to whether the lady would turn round or go straight on </s>
<s> In the latter case, it would not be possible for her to attract her attention </s>
<s> Her heart seemed to stand still with anxiety as she peered over the high wall at the spot where the two roads crossed </s>

<s> He mentioned the fact to his mistress </s>
<s> "Maybe we'd better go back, ma'am," he said </s>
<s> "Maybe we'd better not, John," said the buxom lady </s>
<s> "People can look over their garden walls without our interfering with them, can't they" </s>
<s> "Yes, ma'am, but she was a-hollerin' at us" </s>
<s> "No, John, was she though </s>
<s> Maybe this is a private road and we have no right to be on it" </s>
<s> "She gave a holler as if some one was a-hurtin' of her," said John with decision </s>
<s> "Then we'll go back," said the lady, and turned the pony round </s>
<s> Hence it came about that just as Kate was descending with a sad heart from her post of observation, she was electrified to see the brown pony reappear and come trotting round the curve of the lane, with a rapidity which was altogether foreign to that quadruped's usual habits </s>

<s> I am shut up in these grounds, and shall be murdered unless help comes" </s>

<s> cried the lady in the pony-carriage, dropping back in her seat and raising her hands in astonishment </s>

<s> "My guardian has shut me up here for some weeks, and I firmly believe that he will never let me out alive </s>
<s> Oh, don't, pray don't think me mad </s>
<s> I am as sane as you are, though, God knows, what I have gone through has been enough to shake my reason" </s>
<s> This last appeal of Kate's was in answer to an expression of incredulity and doubt which had passed over the face of the lady below </s>
<s> It was successful in its object, for the ring of truth with which she spoke and the look of anxiety and terror upon her face were too genuine to be mistaken </s>
<s> The lady drew her rein so as to bring the carriage as near the wall as was possible without losing sight of Kate's face </s>
<s> "My dear," she said, "you may safely tell me everything </s>
<s> Whatever I can do to help you shall be done, and where I am powerless there are others who are my friends and may be of assistance </s>
<s> Scully is my name-- Mrs Lavinia Scully, of London </s>
<s> Don't cry, my poor girl, but tell me all about it, and let us see how we can put matters right" </s>
<s> Thus encouraged, Kate wiped away the tears which had been brought to her eyes by the unwonted sound of a friendly voice </s>
<s> Leaning forward as far as she could, and preventing herself from falling by passing her arm round a great branch which shot across the top of the shed, she gave in as few words as she could a detailed account of all that had befallen her </s>
<s> She described her guardian's anxiety that she should marry his son, her refusal, their sudden departure from London, their life at the Priory, the manner in which she was cut off from all human aid, and the reasons which made her believe that an attempt would be made upon her life </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLI </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLII </s>
<s> THE THREE FACES AT THE WINDOW </s>
<s> Late in the afternoon Ezra arrived at the Priory </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLIII </s>
<s> THE BAIT ON THE HOOK </s>
<s> The grey winter evening was beginning to steal in before the details had all been arranged by the conspirators </s>
<s> It had grown so chill that Kate had abandoned her attempt at gardening, and had gone back to her room </s>
<s> Ezra left his father and Burt by the fire and came out to the open hall-door </s>
<s> The grim old trees looked gaunt and eerie as they waved their naked arms about in the cutting wind </s>
<s> A slight fog had come up from the sea and lay in light wreaths over the upper branches, like a thin veil of gauze </s>
<s> Ezra was shivering as he surveyed the dreary scene, when he felt a hand on his arm, and looking round saw that the maid Rebecca was standing beside him </s>
<s> "Haven't you got one word for me" </s>
<s> she said sadly, looking up into his face </s>
<s> "It's but once a week, and then never a word of greeting" </s>
<s> "I didn't see you, my lass," Ezra answered </s>
<s> "How does the Priory suit you" </s>
<s> "One place is the same as another to me," she said drearily </s>
<s> "You asked me to come here, and I have come </s>
<s> You said once that you would let me know how I could serve you down here </s>
<s> When am I to know" </s>
<s> "Why, there's no secret about that </s>
<s> You do serve me when you look after my father as you have done these weeks back </s>
<s> That old woman isn't fit to manage the whole place by herself" </s>
<s> "That wasn't what you meant, though," said the girl, looking at him with questioning eyes </s>

<s> You have something on your mind, and have now, only you keep it to yourself </s>
<s> Why won't you trust me with it" </s>
<s> "Don't be a fool" </s>
<s> answered Ezra curtly </s>
<s> "I have a great deal to worry me in business matters </s>

<s> "Who is that man who has come down" </s>

<s> "I should like to know how long we are to be kept down here, and what the meaning of it all may be" </s>
<s> "We are going back before the end of the winter, and the meaning of it is that Miss Harston was not well and needed a change of air </s>

<s> He was determined to allay as far as possible any suspicions that the girl might have previously formed </s>
<s> "And what brings _you_ down here" </s>
<s> she asked, with the same searching look </s>
<s> "You don't come down into this hole without some good reason </s>

<s> There was a time when you was fond of me" </s>
<s> "So I am now, lass" </s>

<s> "If he was under the sod you would not be the sadder </s>
<s> It's my belief as you come down after that doll-faced missy upstairs" </s>
<s> "Dry up, now" </s>
<s> said Ezra roughly </s>
<s> "I've had enough of your confounded nonsense" </s>
<s> "You don't talk in that style to her," she said excitedly </s>
<s> "You scorn me, but I know this, that if I can't have your love no one else shall </s>
<s> I've got a dash of the gipsy in me, as you know </s>
<s> Rather than that girl should have you, I would knife her and you, too" </s>
<s> She shook her clenched right hand as she spoke, and her face was so full of vindictive passion that Ezra was astonished </s>

<s> The reaction had already come upon her, however, and tears were running down her cheeks </s>
<s> "You'll never leave me entirely" </s>
<s> she cried, clasping his arm </s>
<s> "I could bear to share your love with another, but I wouldn't have you turn altogether against me" </s>
<s> "You'll have my father out presently with your damned noise" </s>
<s> said Ezra </s>
<s> "Get away, and wash your face" </s>
<s> His word was law to her, and she turned away, still weeping bitterly </s>
<s> In her poor, dim, eventless life the sole bright spot had been the attention which the young merchant had occasionally shown her </s>
<s> To her distorted fancy he was a man among men, a hero, all that was admirable and magnificent </s>
<s> What was there which she would not do for him </s>
<s> She had the faithfulness of a dog, but like a dog she would snarl fiercely at any one who came between her master's affection and herself </s>
<s> Deep down in her heart rankled the one suspicion which no assurances could remove, that an understanding existed between the man she loved and the woman she hated </s>
<s> As she withdrew to her room she determined that during this visit of Ezra's she would manage in such a way that no communication could pass between them without her knowledge </s>
<s> She knew that it was a dangerous thing to play the spy upon the young man, for he had shown her before now that her sex was no precaution against his brutality </s>
<s> Nevertheless, she set herself to do it, with all the cunning and perseverance of a jealous woman </s>
<s> As the light faded and the greys of evening deepened into darkness, Kate sat patiently in her bare little room </s>
<s> A coal fire sputtered and sparkled in the rusty grate, and there was a tin bucket full of coals beside the fender from which to replenish it </s>
<s> She was very cold, so she drew her single chair up to the blaze and held her hands over it </s>
<s> It was a lonesome and melancholy vigil, while the wind whistled through the branches of the trees and moaned drearily in the cracks and crannies of the old house </s>
<s> When were her friends coming </s>
<s> Perhaps something had occurred to detain them to-day </s>
<s> This morning such a thing would have appeared to her to be an impossibility, but now that the time had come when she had expected them, it appeared probable enough that something might have delayed them </s>
<s> To-morrow at latest they could not fail to come </s>
<s> She wondered what they would do if they did arrive </s>
<s> Would they come boldly up the avenue and claim her from the Girdlestones, or would they endeavour to communicate with her first </s>
<s> Whatever they decided upon would be sure to be for the best </s>
<s> She went to the window once and looked out </s>
<s> It promised to be a wild night </s>
<s> Far away in the south-west lay a great cumulus of rugged clouds from which dark streamers radiated over the sky, like the advance guard of an army </s>
<s> Here and there a pale star twinkled dimly out through the rifts, but the greater part of the heavens was black and threatening </s>
<s> It was so dark that she could no longer see the sea, but the crashing, booming sound of the great waves filled the air and the salt spray came driving in through the open window </s>
<s> She shut it and resumed her seat by the fire, shivering partly from cold and partly from some vague presentiment of evil </s>
<s> An hour or more had passed when she heard a step upon the stairs and a knock came to her door </s>
<s> It was Rebecca, with a cup of tea upon a tray and some bread-and-butter </s>
<s> Kate was grateful at this attention, for it saved her from having to go down to the dining-room and face Ezra and his unpleasant-looking companion </s>
<s> Rebecca laid down the tray, and then, to her mistress's surprise, turned back and shut the door </s>
<s> The girl's face was very pale, and her manner was wild and excited </s>
<s> "Here's a note for you," she said </s>
<s> "It was given Mrs Jorrocks to give you, but I am better at climbing stairs than she is, so I brought it up" </s>
<s> She handed Kate a little slip of paper as she spoke </s>
<s> A note for her </s>
<s> Could it be that her friends had arrived and had managed to send a message to her </s>
<s> It must be so </s>
<s> She took it from the maid </s>
<s> As she did so she noticed that the other's hands were shaking as though she had the ague </s>
<s> "You are not well, Rebecca," said Kate kindly </s>
<s> "Oh yes, I am </s>
<s> You read your note and don't mind me," the girl answered, in her usual surly fashion </s>
<s> Instead of leaving the room, she was bustling about the bed as though putting things in order </s>
<s> Kate's impatience was too great to allow her to wait, so she untwisted the paper, which had no seal or fastening </s>
<s> She had hoped in her heart to see the name of her lover at the end of it </s>
<s> Instead of that, her eye fell upon the signature of Ezra Girdlestone </s>
<s> What could he have to say to her </s>
<s> She moved the solitary candle on to the mantelpiece, and read the following note, roughly scribbled upon a coarse piece of paper:-- "MY DEAR MISS HARSTON" </s>
<s> "I am afraid your confinement here has been very irksome to you </s>
<s> I have repeatedly requested my father to alleviate or modify it, but he has invariably refused </s>
<s> As he still persists in his refusal, I wish to offer you my aid, and, to show you that I am your sincere friend in spite of all that has passed, it you could slip out to-night at nine o'clock and meet me by the withered oak at the head of the avenue, I shall see you safe to Bedsworth, and you can, if you wish, go on to Portsmouth by the next train </s>
<s> I shall manage so that you may find the door open by that time </s>
<s> I shall not, of course, go to Portsmouth with you, but shall return here after dropping you at the station </s>
<s> I do this small thing to show you that, hopeless as it may be, the affection which I bear you is still as deep as ever" </s>
<s> "Yours," "E </s>
<s> GIRDLESTONE" </s>
<s> Our heroine was so surprised at this epistle that she sat for some time dangling the slip of paper between her fingers and lost in thought </s>
<s> When she glanced round, Rebecca had left the room </s>
<s> She rolled the paper up and threw it into the fire </s>
<s> Ezra, then, was not so hard-hearted as she had thought him </s>
<s> He had used his influence to soften his father </s>
<s> Should she accept this chance of escape, or should she wait some word from her friends </s>
<s> Perhaps they were already in Bedsworth, but did not know how to communicate with her </s>
<s> If so, this offer of Ezra's was just what was needed </s>
<s> In any case, she could go on to Portsmouth and telegraph from there to the Dimsdales </s>
<s> It was too good an offer to be refused </s>
<s> She made up her mind that she would accept it </s>
<s> It was past eight now, and nine was the hour </s>
<s> She stood up with the intention of putting on her cloak and her bonnet </s>
<s> CHAPTER XLIV </s>
<s> THE SHADOW OF DEATH </s>
<s> This conversation with Rebecca had suggested to Ezra that he might still have influence enough with his father's ward to induce her to come out of doors, and so put herself within the reach of Burt </s>
<s> He had proposed the plan to his father, who approved of it heartily </s>

<s> There was evidently only one incentive strong enough to bring it about, and that was the hope of escape </s>
<s> By harping skilfully upon this string they might lure her into the trap </s>

<s> she asked </s>

<s> "Thank ye </s>
<s> Them stairs tries my rheumatiz something cruel" </s>
<s> The maid took the note and carried it upstairs </s>
<s> Instead of taking it straight to her mistress she slipped into her own room and read every word of it </s>

<s> She little dreamed of the struggle which was going on in the dark-eyed girl's mind against the impulse which urged her to seize her imagined rival by the white throat and choke the life out of her </s>
<s> "It's eight o'clock now," Ezra was saying downstairs </s>
<s> "I wonder whether she will come" </s>
<s> "She is sure to come," his father said briefly </s>
<s> "Suppose she didn't" </s>
<s> "In that case we should find other means to bring her out </s>

<s> I can't understand how you look so unconcerned </s>
<s> If you were going to sign an invoice or audit an account or anything else in the way of business you could not take it more calmly </s>
<s> I wish the time would come </s>
<s> This waiting is terrible" </s>
<s> "Let us pass the time to advantage," said John Girdlestone; and drawing a little fat Bible from his pocket he began to read it aloud in a solemn and sonorous voice </s>

<s> "Isn't it time to wake him up" </s>
<s> Ezra asked, interrupting the reading </s>

<s> "What a brute he looks" </s>
<s> he said </s>

<s> The navvy was certainly not a pretty sight </s>

<s> His eyes were half open and looked bleared and unhealthy, while his thick lips puffed out with a whistling sound at every expiration </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLV </s>
<s> THE INVASION OF HAMPSHIRE </s>
<s> When Tom and the major arrived at Waterloo Station, the latter in the breathless condition described in a preceding chapter, they found the German waiting for them with his two fellow-exiles </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLVI </s>
<s> A MIDNIGHT CRUISE </s>
<s> If ever two men were completely cowed and broken down those two were the African merchants and his son </s>
<s> Wet, torn, and soiled, they still struggled on in their aimless flight, crashing through hedges and clambering over obstacles, with the one idea in their frenzied minds of leaving miles between them and that fair accusing face </s>
<s> Exhausted and panting they still battled through the darkness and the storm, until they saw the gleam of the surge and heard the crash of the great waves upon the beach </s>
<s> Then they stopped amid the sand and the shingle </s>
<s> The moon was shining down now in all its calm splendour, illuminating the great tossing ocean and the long dark sweep of the Hampshire coast </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLVIII </s>
<s> CAPTAIN HAMILTON MIGGS SEES A VISION </s>
<s> Ezra Girdlestone had given many indications during his life, both in Africa and elsewhere, of being possessed of the power of grasping a situation and of acting for the best at the shortest notice </s>
<s> He never showed this quality more conclusively than at that terrible moment, when he realized not only that the crime in which he bad participated had failed, but that all was discovered, and that his father and he were hunted criminals </s>
<s> With the same intuitive quickness which made him a brilliant man of business, he saw instantly what were the only available means of escape, and proceeded at once to adopt them </s>
<s> If they could but reach the vessel of Captain Hamilton Miggs they might defy the pursuit of the law </s>
<s> The _Black Eagle_ had dropped down the Thames on the very Saturday which was so fruitful of eventful episodes </s>
<s> Miggs would lie at Gravesend, and intended afterwards to beat round to the Downs, there to await the final instructions of the firm </s>
<s> If they could catch him before he left, there was very little chance that he would know anything of what had occurred </s>
<s> It was a fortunate chance that the next day was Sunday, and there would be no morning paper to enlighten him as to the doings in Hampshire </s>
<s> They had only to invent some plausible excuse for their wish to accompany him, and get him to drop them upon the Spanish coast </s>
<s> Once out of sight of England and on the broad ocean, what detective could follow their track </s>
<s> Of course upon Sampson's return all would come out </s>
<s> Ezra reckoned, however, that it would be some time before the fisherman got back from his journey </s>
<s> What was a favourable wind going would be dead in his teeth coming back </s>
<s> It might take him a week's tacking and beating about before he got home </s>
<s> By that time Ezra hoped to be beyond the reach of all danger </s>
<s> He had a thousand five pound Bank of England notes sewn into the back of his waistcoat, for knowing that a crash might come at any moment, he had long made provision against it </s>

<s> remarked Ezra </s>

<s> Captain Hamilton Miggs had found the liquor of the _Cock and Cowslip_ so very much to his taste, in spite of its vitriolic peculiarities recorded in a preceding chapter, that he rejoined his ship in a very shaky and demoralized condition </s>
<s> He was a devout believer in the homoeopathic revelation that like may be cured by like, so he forthwith proceeded to set himself straight by the consumption of an unlimited quantity of ship's rum </s>
<s> "What's the good of having a pilot aboard if I am to keep sober" </s>
<s> he hiccoughed to his mate McPherson </s>

<s> He was so exhausted by his performance that he fell fast asleep, and snored stertorously for fifteen hours, at the end of which time he came on deck and found that the _Black Eagle_ was lying off Deal, and that her anchor was just being hoisted for a start up Channel </s>
<s> Captain Hamilton Miggs watched the sail-setting with his hands in his pockets, and swore promiscuously at every one, from the mate downwards, in a hearty comprehensive way, which showed a mind that was superior to petty distinctions </s>
<s> Having run over all the oaths that he could think of, he dived below and helped himself from the rum bottle, a process which appeared to aid his memory or his invention, for he reappeared upon deck and evolved a new many-jointed expletive at the man at the wheel </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLIX </s>
<s> A VOYAGE IN A COFFIN SHIP </s>
<s> The early part of the voyage of the _Black Eagle_ was extremely fortunate </s>
<s> The wind came round to the eastward, and wafted them steadily down Channel, until on the third day they saw the Isle of Ushant lying low upon the sky-line </s>
<s> No inquisitive gunboat or lurking police launch came within sight of them, though whenever any vessel's course brought her in their direction the heart of Ezra Girdlestone sank within him </s>
<s> On one occasion a small brig signalled to them, and the wretched fugitives, when they saw the flags run up, thought that all was lost </s>
<s> It proved, however, to be merely some trivial message, and the two owners breathed again </s>
<s> The wind fell away on the day that they cleared the Channel, and the whole surface of the sea was like a great expanse of quicksilver, which shimmered in the rays of the wintry sun </s>
<s> There was still a considerable swell after the recent gale, and the _Black Eagle_ lay rolling about as though she had learned habits of inebriation from her skipper </s>
<s> The sky was very clear above, but all round the horizon a low haze lay upon the water </s>
<s> So silent was it that the creaking of the boats as they swung at the davits, and the straining of the shrouds as the ship rolled, sounded loud and clear, as did the raucous cries of a couple of gulls which hovered round the poop </s>
<s> Every now and then a rumbling noise ending in a thud down below showed that the swing of the ship had caused something to come down with a run </s>
<s> Underlying all other sounds, however, was a muffled clank, clank, which might almost make one forget that this was a sailing ship, it sounded so like the chipping of a propeller </s>
<s> "What is that noise, Captain Miggs" </s>
<s> asked John Girdlestone as he stood leaning over the quarter rail, while the old sea-dog, sextant in hand, was taking his midday observations </s>
<s> The captain had been on his good behaviour since the unexpected advent of his employers, and he was now in a wonderful and unprecedented state of sobriety </s>
<s> "Them's the pumps a-goin'," Miggs answered, packing his sextant away in its case </s>
<s> "The pumps </s>
<s> I thought they were only used when a ship was in danger" </s>

<s> "This ship is in danger," Miggs remarked calmly </s>
<s> "In danger" </s>
<s> cried Ezra, looking round the clear sky and placid sea </s>
<s> "Where is the danger </s>
<s> I did not think you were such an old woman, Miggs" </s>
<s> "We will see about that," the seaman answered angrily </s>

<s> "I mean to tell you that there are places where you could put your fingers through her seams </s>

<s> Even the two landsmen could see now that the danger was no imaginary one, and that a storm was about to burst over them </s>
<s> The long black lines of vapour had lengthened and coalesced, until now the whole northern heaven was one great rolling black cloud, with an angry, ragged fringe which bespoke the violence of the wind that drove it </s>
<s> Here and there against the deep black background a small whitish or sulphur-coloured wreath stood clearly out, looking livid and dangerous </s>
<s> The whole great mass was sweeping onwards with prodigious and majestic rapidity, darkening the ocean beneath it, and emitting a dull, moaning, muttering sound, which was indescribably menacing and mournful </s>
<s> "This may be the same gale as was on some days ago," Miggs remarked </s>
<s> "They travel in circles very often, and come back to where they start from" </s>
<s> "We are all snug aloft, but this ship won't stand much knocking about, an' that's a fact," observed the mate gloomily </s>
<s> It was blowing now in short frequent puffs, which ruffled the surface of the water, and caused the _Black Eagle_ to surge slowly forward over the rollers </s>
<s> A few drops of rain came pattering down upon the deck </s>
<s> The great bank of cloud was above the ship, still hurrying wildly across the heavens </s>
<s> "Look out" </s>
<s> cried an old quartermaster </s>
<s> "Here she comes" </s>
<s> As he spoke the storm burst with a shriek, as though all the demons of the air had been suddenly unchained and were rejoicing in their freedom </s>
<s> The force of the blast was so great that Girdlestone could almost have believed that he had been struck by some solid object </s>
<s> The barque heeled over until her lee rail touched the water, and lay so for a minute or more in a smother of foam </s>
<s> Her deck was at such an angle that it seemed as though she never could right herself </s>
<s> Gradually, however, she rose a little, staggered and trembled like a living thing, and then plunged away through the storm, as a piece of paper is whirled before the wind </s>
<s> By evening the gale was at its height </s>
<s> The _Black Eagle_ was running under maintopsail and foretopmast staysail </s>
<s> The sea had risen very quickly, as it will when wind comes upon a swell </s>
<s> As far as the eye could see from the summit of a wave there was a vista of dark towering ridges with their threatening crests of foam </s>

<s> Once or twice waves actually broke over the vessel, crashing and roaring down the deck, and washing hither and thither until gradually absorbed between the planks or drained away through the scupper-holes </s>

<s> WINDS UP THE THREAD AND TIES TWO KNOTS AT THE END </s>
<s> Great was the excitement of the worthy couple at Phillimore Gardens when Kate Harston was brought back to them </s>
<s> Good Mrs Dimsdale pressed her to her ample bosom and kissed her, and scolded her, and wept over her, while the doctor was so moved that it was only by assuming an expression of portentous severity and by bellowing and stamping about that he was able to keep himself in decent control </s>
<s> "And you really thought we had forgotten you because we were insane enough to stop writing at that villain's request" </s>
<s> he said, patting Kate's pale cheeks tenderly and kissing her </s>
<s> "I was very foolish," she said, blushing prettily and rearranging her hair, which had been somewhat tumbled by her numerous caresses </s>
<s> "Oh, that scoundrel--that pair of scoundrels" </s>
<s> roared the doctor, shaking his fist and dancing about on the hearth-rug </s>
<s> "Pray God they may catch 'em before the trial comes off" </s>
<s> The good physician's prayer was not answered in this case, for Burt was the only criminal who appeared in the dock </s>
<s> Our friends all went down to the Winchester Assizes to give evidence, and the navvy was duly convicted of the death of Rebecca Taylforth and condemned to death </s>
<s> He was executed some three weeks afterwards, dying as he had lived, stolid and unrepenting </s>
<s> There is a little unpretending church not far from Phillimore Gardens, in which a little unpretending clergyman preaches every Sunday out of a very shabby pulpit </s>
<s> It lies in Castle Lane, which is a narrow by-way, and the great crowd of church-goers ebbs and flows within a hundred yards of it, but none know of its existence, for it has never risen to the dignity of a spire, and the bell is so very diminutive that the average muffin man produces quite as much noise </s>
<s> Hence, with the exception of some few families who have chanced to find their way there, and have been so pleased with their spiritual welcome that they have returned, there is a poor and fluctuating congregation </s>
<s> So scanty is it that the struggling incumbent could very well weep when he has spent the week in polishing and strengthening his sermon, and then finds upon the Sunday how very scanty is the audience to whom it is to be addressed </s>
<s> Imagine, then, this good man's surprise when asked to publish the banns of marriage of two couples simultaneously, each of whom he knew to be in the upper circles of life, and when informed at the same time that the said marriages were actually to be celebrated under his own auspices and in his own church </s>
<s> In the fullness of his heart he at once bought a most unwearable black bonnet with lilac flowers and red berries, which he brought in triumph to his wife, who, good woman, affected extreme delight, and afterwards cut away all the obnoxious finery and replaced it to her own taste </s>
<s> The scanty congregation was no less surprised when they heard that Tobias Clutterbuck, bachlelor, was about to marry Lavinia Scully, widow, and that Thomas Dimsdale, bachelor, was to do as much to Catherine Harston, spinster </s>
<s> They communicated the tidings to their friends, and the result was a great advertisement to the little church, so that the incumbent preached his favourite sermon upon barren fig trees to a crowded audience, and received such an offertory as had never entered into his wildest dreams </s>

<s> These gentlemen grouped themselves at the end of the church conversing in low whispers and looking exceedingly uncomfortable, as is the prerogative of the sterner sex under such circumstances </s>

<s> Dimsdale too, with the brightest of smiles and snowiest of waistcoats, giving away the brides in the most open-handed fashion </s>

<s> The liabilities of the firm of Girdlestone proved to be less serious than was at first imagined </s>
<s> After the catastrophe which had befallen the founder of the business, there was almost a panic in Fenchurch Street, but on examination it proved that though the books had been deliberately falsified for some time, yet trade had been so brisk of late that, with a little help, the firm could continue to exist </s>
<s> Dimsdale threw all his money and his energy into the matter, and took Gilray into partnership, which proved to be an excellent thing for both of them </s>
<s> The firm of Dimsdale and Gilray is now among the most successful and popular of all the English firms connected with the African trade </s>
<s> Of their captains there is none upon whom they place greater reliance than upon McPherson, whose boat was providentially saved from the danger which destroyed his former captain and his employer </s>
<s> What became of Ezra Girdlestone was never known </s>
<s> Some years after Tom heard from a commercial traveller of a melancholy, broken man who haunted the low betting-houses of San Francisco, and who met his death eventually in some drunken fracas </s>
<s> There was much about this desperado which tallied with the description of young Girdlestone, but nothing certain was ever known about the matter </s>
<s> And now I must bid adieu to the shadowy company with whom I have walked so long </s>
<s> I see them going on down the vista of the future, gathering wisdom and happiness as they go </s>
<s> There is the major, as stubby-toed and pigeon-breasted as ever, broken from many of his Bohemian ways, but still full of anecdote and of kindliness </s>
<s> There is his henchman, Von Baumser, too, who is a constant diner at his hospitable board, and who conveys so many sweets to a young Clutterbuck who has made his appearance, that one might suspect him of receiving a commission from the family doctor </s>
<s> Mrs Clutterbuck, as buxom and pleasant as ever, makes noble efforts at stopping these contraband supplies, but the wily Teuton still manages to smuggle them through in the face of every obstacle </s>
<s> I see Kate and her husband, chastened by their many troubles, and making the road to the grave pleasant to the good old couple who are so proud of their son </s>
<s> All these I watch as they pass away into the dim coming time, and I know as I shut the book that, whatever may be in store for us there, they, at least, can never in the eternal justice of things come to aught but good </s>
<s> THE END </s>
